CI: `DownloadNotificationsTest` (channel/ForegroundInfo); foreground/notification behavior device-bound → `VERIFICATION.md §L5–L6`. (bge foreground wiring left optional — it's a 34 MB fetch.)
- [x] **CHECKPOINT UX2:** `./gradlew build` green; feedback/selection/swipe/organize/monitor/notification suites pass; no payload/export change (PayloadBuilder/redaction structural tests still pass); device-bound items recorded in `VERIFICATION.md §L`. Ships on the v2.0-alpha line.

## Phase F2 — On-device chat fix (post-v2.0-alpha device run, 2026-06-19)

> First on-device test of P2 chat (S20, from an Android bug report) showed per-paper Ask **and** collection chat returning blank answers + "Couldn't get an answer." Root-caused from logcat: `GemmaEngine.SPEC` pointed at the **WebGPU-only** `gemma-4-E2B-it-web.litertlm`, whose single `gpu_artisan` decoder has no CPU `TF_LITE_PREFILL_DECODE` graph — on the CPU backend (NPU registration fails) it loads but generates zero tokens. No cloud provider configured, so chat resolves to on-device.

- [x] F2.1 Swap `GemmaEngine.SPEC` to the standard CPU/GPU build `gemma-4-E2B-it.litertlm` (2.59 GB, SHA `18193810…63c`); docs (`on-device-ai.md`) + `VERIFICATION.md §J5/§J6/§K3/§L5` updated; `GemmaSpecTest` guards against regressing to a `-web` build.
- [x] F2.2 Treat a zero-token generation as a failure: `GemmaEngine`/`NanoEngine` throw `AiException` when a stream produces no tokens (was: clean `Done` → silent blank bubble persisted as COMPLETE); `AskViewModel` also guards an empty `Done` (covers cloud providers). Tests: `AskViewModelTest` empty-completion → error.
- [x] F2.3 "Test connection" truthfulness rides F2.2 (an empty on-device ping now throws → `ConnectionTest.Error`).
- [x] F2.4 `ModelDownloader` purges stale same-extension siblings on (re)download, so the swap doesn't strand the old ~2 GB `-web` file; extension-scoped so the bge `.onnx` is untouched. Test: `ModelDownloaderTest` cleanup.
- [x] F2.5 Empty/failed on-device generation now surfaces the error toast instead of a blank bubble (the user-visible win; messaging reuses `ask_error_generic`).
- [E] **CHECKPOINT F2:** `./gradlew build` green; the root fix is **emulator-verified** (V3, 2026-06-26, 6 GB AVD — `VERIFICATION.md` log + §J5/§J6/§J7/§K3): the standard 2.59 GB `gemma-4-E2B-it.litertlm` downloads + SHA-verifies, the engine loads on **CPU** with no `TF_LITE_PREFILL_DECODE` skip, Test connection returns a reply, and per-paper Ask streams **real grounded tokens, not a blank bubble** (the F2 regression is closed — collection chat shares the same `GemmaEngine`, so the token-generation fix covers it). **Remaining (true device, the S20):** arm64/NPU throughput, the old-`-web`-model **purge** on re-download (this AVD had no stale sibling), the **forced-failure** path on device (zero-token → error toast; unit-tested via `AskViewModelTest`), and a collection-scope on-device run.

## Phase P-Rich — Rich AI output & rendering (v2-era, user-directed 2026-06-23)

> Elevate AI answers from plain text into rich, illustrative, navigable output — markdown, math, diagrams/charts, export/share — so the assistant can explain dense research the way papers do, and chat becomes a first-class surface. Built docs-first per `docs/SPEC-RICH-OUTPUT.md`. Local + offline + no-telemetry throughout (rich blocks render from bundled assets). MDX rejected (JS runtime + arbitrary-component execution); fenced blocks (` ```mermaid `/` ```math `/` ```chart `/` ```svg `) give the same power safely. Provider-aware: cloud gets the full format invitation, on-device Gemma degrades to plain markdown. Tiered.

- [x] **R0 — markdown + clickable citations + spec.** `SPEC-RICH-OUTPUT.md`; `commonmark-java` parser + a custom `MarkdownText` Compose AST renderer (bold/italic/headings/lists/**tables**/code/links; fenced info-string = the R1/R2 routing hook; remote images off); render assistant answers in `AskBubble`; thread the assembler's labeled context (`[n] → {paperId, excerpt}`) to the assistant message → tappable `[n]` + a "Sources" expander; markdown system-prompt invitation. **Emulator-verified 2026-06-23** (`VERIFICATION.md` log): real markdown incl. a bordered table renders, `[1]` taps to Sources. **Gemini J3 fixed:** the pinned `gemini-2.0-flash` is deprecated (HTTP 404 → generic "couldn't reach"); swapped to `gemini-2.5-flash` (Gemini was fully broken before this).
- [x] **R1 — math.** Sandboxed offline `RichBlockWebView` (KaTeX bundled; all network/file access blocked; talks back only via `arxiver://cite|height` link interception — no JS↔app data bridge) + a `RichHtml` builder (commonmark `HtmlRenderer` → HTML → KaTeX); a math-containing answer renders **whole** through it (so inline `$…$` works), plain answers stay on the native R0 renderer; provider-aware **cloud-only** math system-prompt invitation. **Emulator-verified 2026-06-23:** a display equation (`Ŝ = Σ wₖxₖ`) + inline math in a table/headings render correctly, themed, and **still render in airplane mode** (offline, from bundled assets). `jlatexmath` rejected (dep-risk); WebView chosen as the R2 foundation.
- [x] **R2 — diagrams (Mermaid).** Bundled `mermaid@10.9.3` (UMD) on the R1 `RichBlockWebView`; `RichHtml` rewrites ` ```mermaid ` → `<pre class="mermaid">` and runs Mermaid (`securityLevel:'strict'`, theme matched to light/dark) after KaTeX; `RichContent.has` routes diagram answers; cloud system-prompt invites Mermaid (flowchart/sequence/mindmap/timeline + pie/xychart charts). Charts = Mermaid's native types (no extra dep). **Emulator-verified 2026-06-23:** a flowchart renders as a real diagram (styled nodes + arrows), in **light AND dark** theme, and **still renders in airplane mode** (offline, bundled Mermaid). **Raw ` ```svg ` deferred to R2.5** (model-SVG sanitization is its own surface; Mermaid covers the bulk).
- [x] **R2.5 — sanitized raw ` ```svg `** on the same WebView (strip script/event-handlers/foreignObject/external refs). → **DELIVERED as Phase P-Share PS.1** (jsoup-sanitized + actually *rendered*; P-Share checkpoint `[x]`). *(Box healed 2026-07-11 — the reshaped work shipped; this was a stale pointer.)*
- [x] **R3a — navigation & capture.** Tappable `arXiv:NNNN.NNNNN` (+ legacy) cross-references that open the paper **in-app** (validated via `ArxivId.parse`, fetch-on-demand if not in-library) — wired in **both** render paths: native `MarkdownText` (a `crossRef`-tinted `LinkAnnotation`, distinct from `[n]` citations) and the WebView (`RichHtml` emits `<a href="arxiver://paper/<id>">`, intercepted in `RichBlockWebView`; legacy slash-ids percent-encoded to one path segment). Plus **pin-answer-to-notes**: a settled assistant answer pins into the paper's notes via `LibraryRepository.addNote` with an "Added to notes" snackbar; hidden for collection-scope chat (no single paper). Cross-refs/pin ride existing callbacks (`onPaperClick`, `addNote`) — no new deps, no prompt change, redaction goldens untouched. Pin shows an **in-sheet** "Added to notes ✓" confirmation (the app snackbar sits behind the modal). **Emulator-verified 2026-06-24** (`VERIFICATION.md`): a grounded answer's `arXiv:2606.23597` renders as a tertiary-tinted link (distinct from `[n]`), tapping it dismisses the sheet and opens the paper; verified **light + dark**; pin flips to "Added to notes ✓" in-sheet; no crashes. WebView-path cross-refs covered by unit tests + the proven R1/R2 `arxiver://` interception.
- [x] **R3c — Ask preset library (text-only).** Extensible `AskPresets` registry of 9 one-tap research tools (Summarize is member #1, reusing its exact prompt; + Key contributions, Explain method, Limitations, Compare related, Explain simply, Key terms, BibTeX, Reproducibility). **A preset is just a predefined question** — tapping a chip runs its model-facing instruction through the existing `ask()` path, so the answer is grounded + cited and the request is byte-identical to a typed question → **zero `ChatContextAssembler` change, redaction goldens untouched**. UI: a horizontally-scrollable `AssistChip` row above the input, always available, **scope-filtered** (`forScope(scope is Paper)` drops paper-only presets like BibTeX/Reproducibility in collection chat) and disabled while a turn streams. The "what" dimension. **Emulator-verified 2026-06-24** (`VERIFICATION.md`): the chip row renders + scrolls; tapping **Key contributions** on a paper produced a structured cited answer, with the privacy preview showing the preset instruction as the `Question:` and the **system prompt unchanged**; collection scope correctly hid the paper-only presets.
- [x] **R3b — 3-mode depth dial.** `ChatMode` (Quick / Standard / Max) as a `SingleChoiceSegmentedButtonRow` in the Ask sheet, default Standard. The mode becomes a short directive **prepended to the user turn** in `ChatContextAssembler.userTurn()` (never the system prompt) — **Standard = empty = byte-identical request → goldens untouched**; Quick = "2–3 sentences"; Max = "thorough/detailed, synthesize, surface nuances" + a **cloud-only** "use a table/Mermaid when it clarifies" nudge (mirroring the rich-invite gate, so on-device Gemma isn't pushed toward broken markup). Applies to typed questions **and** R3c presets (both flow through `ask()`), giving the preset × mode grid. The "how" dimension — orthogonal to presets (audience stays a preset, never a mode facet). **Emulator-verified 2026-06-24** (`VERIFICATION.md`): the segmented control renders (Standard default); selecting **Max** + asking showed the privacy preview prepending the Max directive **incl.** the rich nudge to the `USER` turn with the `SYSTEM` prompt **unchanged**. **Follow-up chips (heuristic + model-gen-in-Max) → R3b.2.**
- [x] **R3b.2 — follow-up suggestion chips.** Tappable next-question chips below a settled answer. **Heuristic** (Quick/Standard/on-device): a pure `FollowUpHeuristics` generator picks 2–3 from a curated template set, de-duped against the asked question + prior session turns, with a true floor backstop and a non-English guard. **Model-generated** (cloud-Max only): `MAX_FOLLOWUPS_SUFFIX` asks for a final `FOLLOWUPS::` line; the shared pure `extractFollowUps` strips it (final-line-only, never mid-answer) from **both** the displayed body and the persisted DB content, falling back to heuristics if absent. Chips re-enter `ask()` via `runPreset` on tap; rendered only on the latest assistant turn, gated `!streaming && !error`. No prompt/golden impact for Standard (suffix rides the user turn, cloud-Max only). Designed via an Ultracode workflow (parallel designers → synthesis → adversarial stress-test that caught 2 ship-blockers: pin the mode through `confirmSend`→`startStream`, and final-line-only extraction). **Emulator-verified 2026-06-24** (`VERIFICATION.md`): Standard showed heuristic chips (method de-duped after a "how does…" question), tapping re-asked it; **Max showed paper-specific model chips** with the sentinel stripped (no leak) and even composed a Mermaid summary diagram.
- **R3d — multimodal "with figures" (vision, cloud-only)** — the "with what input" axis; surfaces as a `requiresVision` preset. Designed via an Ultracode workflow into 4 trust-boundary phases (stress-test caught 8 must-fixes carried forward):
  - [x] **R3d.1 — multimodal request model + provider serialization + `vision` capability** (core:ai only, zero runtime effect). `ChatImage(mediaType, base64, label?)` + `ChatMessage.images` (default empty → text turns byte-identical) + `ProviderCapability.vision`. Anthropic content becomes a `JsonElement` — a JSON **string** for text-only (byte-identical), a text+image **block array** when images present; Gemini keeps its unconditional text `GenPart` + appends `inlineData` parts. `vision=true` for Claude/Gemini, false on-device. `label` never hits the wire. Unit-verified: text-only byte-identity + mixed-content serialization + label-not-on-wire for both providers; **no device surface yet** (vision E2E lands with R3d.4).
  - [x] **R3d.2 — PDF page → downscaled base64.** Injected `PageImageSource` (interface + `PdfPageImageSource` impl + DI). A fresh framework `PdfRenderer` per call on IO, `eraseColor(WHITE)` (JPEG has no alpha → no black-behind-figures, M5), pure `cappedSize` long-edge cap ≤1568px (m4), JPEG q80 `Base64.NO_WRAP`. **Network-free** local-PDF lookup by **globbing** `filesDir/pdfs/<id>v*.pdf` (M1 — no `PaperRepository.paper()` metadata fetch, so the vision path never hits the arXiv limiter). Dead code until R3d.4; pure `cappedSize` math unit-tested; the live `PdfRenderer` render is emulator-verified at R3d.4 where it's reachable.
  - [x] **R3d.3 — privacy-preview disclosure + assembler/repo plumbing.** Optional `attachment: ChatImage?` through `prepare()`→`assemble()`, folded onto the final user turn; `ChatPreviewBuilder` discloses "[Attached image: page N of arXiv:… — image/jpeg, ~KB]" in **both** `text` and `json`, never the base64 (sentinel-base64 golden); assembler refuses to attach when `capability.vision == false`; prepare drops the image if the resolved provider lacks vision. **No device surface yet** (dead code until R3d.4) — disclosure + non-vision-drop + null-attachment byte-identity are unit-verified (ChatContextAssemblerTest ×3 + a sentinel-base64 ChatPreviewBuilderTest); a default-mode/null-attachment call stays byte-identical so the redaction goldens are untouched.
  - [x] **R3d.4 — `requiresVision` preset + gating + page-pick UI.** "Summarize with figures" (`AskPreset.requiresVision`, PAPER scope) gated at sheet-open on (resolved provider `capability.vision` AND a local PDF via `pageCountIfLocal`); 1-based page-pick stepper (default 1); `runVisionPreset` converts 1→0-based once (m1), guards paper scope (m2), re-checks vision at action time (`ask_error_no_vision` if a non-vision provider won mid-sheet — SB1), renders network-free, and re-enters the same `prepare(attachment=…)` → confirm → stream path via shared `handlePrepared`. `forScope(isPaper, visionAvailable=false)` keeps text callers byte-identical (m3). Ultracode-designed (3 lenses → synthesis → adversarial stress-test caught SB1 silent-degrade + SB2 attachment-assertion gap). On-device vision E2E recorded in the `VERIFICATION.md` log.
- [x] **R4 — save / export / share (text/Markdown).** Share a single answer **or** the whole conversation as Markdown via the OS share sheet — a per-answer "Share" button next to Pin, and a "Share this conversation" header action. A pure `ConversationMarkdown` serializer (in-memory `AskMessage` list → `# scope` / `## You` / `## Assistant` + `### Sources` + footer) reusing the existing `ACTION_SEND`+`EXTRA_TEXT` pattern (new `Context.shareText` helper) — **no FileProvider, no manifest/dep change**. Wired in all three Ask hosts (paper, collection, history). Designed via an Ultracode workflow; the stress-test pinned the scope (text-only; image/PDF → R4.2), caught that `ChatHistoryScreen` had no callback wiring to mirror (C-1), that share must read `message.text` not the rendered `body` + the serializer must defensively strip a `FOLLOWUPS::` sentinel (C-2/M-3), and that one shared `truncateExcerpt` helper must back both on-screen Sources and the export (M-2). Red lines held: user-initiated, OS-sheet only, no upload, key never involved, and chat content is **never** routed through the importable backup schema. **Emulator-verified 2026-06-24:** the chooser opens above the sheet with a full, correct Markdown transcript (LaTeX/tables/mermaid bodies, footer), no sentinel leak. **Resumed-history turns carry inline `[n]` without a Sources block** (citations are live-only, not persisted) — documented limitation; **markdown shares as `text/plain`** so non-markdown recipients show raw syntax.
- [x] **R4.2 — rendered image / PDF export.** Export an answer / diagram as PNG/PDF (needs a FileProvider + `EXTRA_STREAM`, emulator-only verification). The WebView path (KaTeX/Mermaid) needs a capture spike — prefer `createPrintDocumentAdapter()`→PDF over an off-screen `drawToBitmap` (the `arxiver://height` async-render race is genuinely flaky). FileProvider authority `${applicationId}.fileprovider` (distinct from `.androidx-startup`). → **DELIVERED as Phase P-Share PS.4a/4b** — the Ultracode judge-panel web-verified that print-adapter fires on `onPageFinished` (HTML loaded, *not* JS-rendered), so it doesn't actually beat the race; PS.4 shipped a **signaled off-screen WebView → PNG** instead (P-Share checkpoint `[x]`). *(Box healed 2026-07-11 — stale pointer.)*
- [x] **R4-TTS — read-aloud.** Speak an answer (aligns with the planned P3 `TextToSpeech`), reading the text alternative for rich blocks. → **DELIVERED as Phase P-Share PS.2** (relocated into the PS.3 per-bubble action row; P-Share checkpoint `[x]`). *(Box healed 2026-07-11 — stale pointer.)*
- [x] **CHECKPOINT P-Rich:** CI green per tier (every R-tier merged green; the R3d.4 PR #47 ran a full `Build, test, lint` in 8m23s); **rich blocks render offline** with text alternatives (R1 KaTeX + R2 Mermaid both verified in airplane mode 2026-06-23; the native `MarkdownText` renderer is the offline-safe fallback for plain answers); **redaction goldens green** (`ChatPreviewBuilderTest` / `PayloadBuilderTest` — the R3d vision path keeps a no-attachment turn byte-identical, and a sent image is disclosed by label/mime/KB, never the base64); **device checks recorded in `VERIFICATION.md`** (R0–R4 + R3d.4 vision E2E, all `[E]`). **Shipped tiers:** R0 (markdown + citations) · R1 (math) · R2 (diagrams/charts) · R3a (cross-refs + pin) · R3c (presets) · R3b (modes) · R3b.2 (follow-ups) · R3d.1–.4 (vision) · R4 (share). **Deferred to backlog** (post-checkpoint follow-ons, non-blocking): R2.5 (raw `svg` sanitizer), R4.2 (image/PDF export + FileProvider), R4-TTS (read-aloud).

## Phase P-Atlas — "the app draws the structure of knowledge; the AI narrates it" (v2-era, user-directed 2026-06-26)

> Elevate AI output from *text the model emits* to *structure the app draws*. The keystone: app-composed, deterministic, always-valid knowledge graphs (citation/similarity/neighbor) from data the app already owns (embeddings + citation edges) — rendered through the existing offline `RichBlockWebView`, narrated by whatever AI is present, working on **every tier including none + airplane mode**. Two enabling threads: a per-engine **richness ladder** (capable on-device models earn tables/diagrams; tiny models stay plain) and a **light on-device tier** (Qwen3-0.6B) for device breadth/speed. Research-grounded (programmatic diagrams beat LLM-emitted, which fail 15–20% of syntax checks — MermaidSeqBench/StructEval; GraphRAG > LLM-only). Designed via an Ultracode workflow (3 vision stances → synthesis → adversarial stress-test, which caught 3 code-verified issues now baked in). Plan: `.claude/plans/` P-Atlas. Red lines hold: artifacts bypass the wire (redaction goldens untouched); on-device sends nothing; one new pinned+SHA model URL (PA.3).

- [x] **PA.1 — RelationGraphBuilder + app-drawn relation graph (keystone; model-independent; every tier, offline).** Pure `RelationGraphBuilder` in `:core:search` (RelationGraph → valid Mermaid: node cap ~12, in-library/external/center distinction, escaped labels matching the WebView's `securityLevel:'strict'`). A `RelationGraphRepository` feeder reuses the Phase-4.9 relations primitives (`embeddingDao.neighborsFor`/`byPaperId`, `citationDao.observeReferences/observeCitations`, `VectorIndex.topK`, `dotSimilarity`). A new `ChatRepository.insertArtifactTurn` persists a complete USER+ASSISTANT turn with **no provider call** (the "no-LLM insert" path didn't exist — stress-test #1); `AskViewModel.runGraphArtifact` mirrors it into UI. A `map_relations` `AskPreset` (artifact, PAPER scope) routes to it. Designed empty states per sparse-data cause (not-embedded / no-relations — stress-test #2). Renders via unchanged `RichContent.has`/`RichBlockWebView`. **Emulator-verified 2026-06-26** (`VERIFICATION.md` log): a valid deterministic graph (center hexagon + cosine-weighted neighbours) generated with **no provider call** and rendered **in airplane mode**. Same-day legibility fix: the builder uses **`graph LR`** (a star fans out tall+narrow, fitting phone width legibly) — re-verified readable; collection-scale level-of-detail + a pannable canvas remain PA.5.
- [x] **PA.0 — SPIKE (non-code; gates PA.3/PA.4).** Kill-criteria + findings (2026-06-26; deep web/arXiv/HF research + primary-source verification). **(a) Gemma E2B rich-output ceiling — DONE** (PA.0a, `VERIFICATION.md` K9): valid grounded Markdown tables with the 1-shot exemplar, no LaTeX/Mermaid. **(b) Light-tier model — NOT BLOCKED:** `litert-community/Qwen3-0.6B` ships a **CPU-capable `Qwen3-0.6B.litertlm` (614 MB, INT8)**, community-benchmarked decoding on CPU (~212 prefill / 13 decode tok/s) — *not* a `-web`/GPU build. ⚠️ The repo also ships `Qwen3-0.6B.mediatek.mt6993.litertlm` (1.2 GB, **NPU-only** — the F2-trap analog) + an INT4 `qwen3_0_6b_mixed_int4.litertlm` (498 MB) fallback → **pin by exact filename + SHA**, never the repo loosely. The empirical "loads + emits tokens in *our* wrapper" leg folds into PA.3's QwenEngine bring-up (`VERIFICATION.md` PA.0b, `[E]`-pending; community CPU benchmarks make it high-confidence). **(c) Constrained decoding — SETTLED, NOT available from Kotlin:** LiteRT-LM's C++ API has LLGuidance (JSON-schema/Lark/regex) but the **Kotlin binding does not surface it** (`SamplerConfig`=topK/topP/temp/seed only; the lone lever is an experimental boolean for *tool-call* syntax) — tracked upstream as **open issue [#1662](https://github.com/google-ai-edge/LiteRT-LM/issues/1662)**, no timeline, and the C++ stack is *widening* the gap (NPU/GPU PRs, no Kotlin). **Decision (gates PA.4):** constrained decoding is rejected as the *wrong tool*, not merely unavailable — at our scale it trades content for syntax ("Constraint Tax" 2026 on Qwen-0.5B/1.5B: validity→100% but accuracy 19.7%→11.0%, wrong-but-valid 49.5%→88.9%; "Let Me Speak Freely?" arXiv:2408.02442). **PA.4 pivots to "app-draws-the-structure"** (see below). Findings → `.claude/memory/` + `VERIFICATION.md`.
- [x] **PA.2 — per-engine richness ladder (PLAIN/STRUCTURED/FULL).** `OutputRichness` is an **abstract** `val` on `OnDeviceEngine` (Gemma=STRUCTURED, Nano=PLAIN) and a **non-defaulted** field on `ProviderCapability` (forcing every construction to declare it — the compiler caught all 4 cloud-capability builders that must say FULL, killing the silent-PLAIN footgun the stress-test flagged). Resolution is **Option B** (a refinement of the original "eager-resolve-reused-by-`chat()`"): `OnDeviceProvider.resolveRichness()` runs the **same** `pickReadyEngine()` as `chat()`, and `ChatRepository.prepare` overrides the on-device capability (`copy(richness=…)`) before assembling — the microscopic prepare-vs-stream readiness flip is **confirmed benign** (STRUCTURED differs from PLAIN only by a table nudge, and the base prompt invites tables for *every* engine), so the heavier Option-A engine-binding is unneeded. The one `ChatContextAssembler` gate widened to 3 states (PLAIN=base; STRUCTURED=base + an **exemplar-backed** table nudge, **no LaTeX/Mermaid**; FULL=cloud, byte-identical). **Research-driven scope:** the 1-shot table example moved *into* PA.2 STRUCTURED (the one lever that lifts ~2B table validity, per 2025–2026 research) — Mermaid (~60% valid) + LaTeX (~9.7% error) stay cloud-only; valid-by-construction (constrained decoding) is **PA.4**. Cloud redaction goldens green; on-device-PLAIN unchanged. **PA.0a (both halves done):** the RAG-budget half is a **headless CI test** (the ~50-token nudge drops no chunk at the 4096 on-device budget); the table-validity half is **`[E]`-verified** (`VERIFICATION.md` K9, 2026-06-26) — Gemma E2B emitted a **valid 2×2 Markdown table** for a comparison question in Standard mode while staying grounded (cited `[1]`, refused to fabricate a comparison the abstract lacks) and emitting no LaTeX/Mermaid. Depends PA.1.
- **PA.3 — light on-device tier (Qwen3-0.6B), `richness=PLAIN` [PA.0b clear].** An **additive** tier aimed at the **3–4 GB device segment** that today falls through to Nano (≤256-tok, too tight for summaries) or cloud-or-nothing — *not* a "smaller Gemma" (on a Gemma-capable device, a 0.6B tier is strictly worse). Split into 3a (plumbing) + 3b (UI):
  - [x] **PA.3a — light-tier inference plumbing (`:core`/DI; the tier works when the model is present).** `InferenceTier.LIGHT`; a `QwenEngine` cloning `GemmaEngine` (incl. the zero-token guard), `tier=LIGHT`, `richness=PLAIN`, `SPEC` pinned to **`litert-community/Qwen3-0.6B` → `Qwen3-0.6B.litertlm` (614 MB, INT8, sha `5555…b0b4`)** by exact filename + SHA — `QwenEngineTest` guards against the `.mediatek` NPU-only sibling (the F2-trap analog). A `@QwenModel` `ModelDownloader` in a **separate `models/light` dir** (the extension-scoped `deleteStaleSiblings` would otherwise have the two `.litertlm` files purge each other). `DeviceCapability.lightReady`/`lightEligible` on `LIGHT_RAM_FLOOR_MB=3072` (user-chosen; below Gemma's 4096), probed by `AndroidDeviceCapabilityProbe`; `TierSelector.fallbackOrder` = Gemma→**LIGHT**→Nano→cloud→none; `QwenEngine` appended to `OnDeviceProvider` engines. **PLAIN genuinely means plain** (research: 0.6B + exemplar ≈ 40–75% table validity — *don't* push tables here). Tests: `QwenEngineTest` (SPEC pin + tier/richness), `TierSelectorTest` (LIGHT ordering), `DeviceCapabilityTest` (lower floor). Empirical CPU-load → `VERIFICATION.md` K10 `[E]`-pending.
  - [x] **PA.3b — light-tier download/manage UI (user-downloadable).** A `LightModelWorker` (`@QwenModel`, foreground-service download with its own progress notification) + `SyncScheduler.downloadLightModel()`; `DefaultOnDeviceModelController` generalized to take an `enqueueDownload` lambda so one class serves both models, with two **qualified** providers (`@GemmaModel`/`@QwenModel`). The settings ViewModel injects both controllers, gains `OnDeviceInfo.lightState`/`lightEligible`, restructures the `combine` (pre-combine the two model states → stays within the 5-arg overload), and dispatches `downloadModel(tier)`/`deleteModel(tier)`. The screen extracts a reusable `ModelCard` rendered for Gemma **and** Qwen, tier-parameterized download callbacks (a `pendingDownloadTier` carries the choice across the notif-permission result), a **LIGHT prefer-chip** (chips now show per-ready-tier when ≥2 are ready), and `isUsable` includes the light tier. The light download is a first-class **background task** (`TaskKind.LIGHT_DOWNLOAD` in `BackgroundTaskMonitor` — listed, cancellable, retryable). Tests: VM tier-dispatch (GEMMA vs LIGHT controller) + light state/eligibility surfacing; `BackgroundTaskMonitorTest` LIGHT mapping; light/dark preview updated. Device run → `VERIFICATION.md` K10 (download Qwen, CPU-load, prefer-LIGHT stream).
- [x] **PA.4 — STRUCTURED valid-by-construction via "app-draws-the-structure".** Extends PA.1's deterministic-artifact thesis to **tables**: the STRUCTURED tier emits a **low-syntax intermediate** (a `TABLE::` … `::TABLE` fence, one row per line, cells split by the composite sentinel **`~|~`** — collision-proof vs math `|x|`/code/markdown — `[n]` citations kept inline) and a pure `:core:ai` **`StructuredTableTransform`** parses it into a `ComparisonTable(header, rows, parseConfidence)` and deterministically renders a **guaranteed-valid GFM table**, or — below a `CONFIDENCE_FLOOR=0.70` gate (`parseConfidence = s·(0.55·rowShapeOk + 0.30·fillRate + 0.15·groundRate)`, `s=0` when <2 cols / no rows) — a **grounded bulleted list** (the ~1B "table reversal", arXiv:2412.17189). Designed via an Ultracode workflow (4 Explore agents mapped the splice/prompt/render/richness surfaces → 3 diverse designs → synthesized blueprint). **Splice:** a shared `settleStructured(prepared, body)` helper applies the transform **iff `prepared.richness == STRUCTURED`** (new `PreparedChat.richness` field) at BOTH the persist seam (`ChatRepository.stream` Done) and the display seam (`AskViewModel.settleFollowUps`), composing *after* `extractFollowUps` — so DB == UI == export, and **cloud FULL / the PLAIN tier are byte-identical** (no-op; a body with no `TABLE::` fence returns unchanged → redaction goldens untouched). Pure, offline, idempotent, no model call → fully off-device golden-tested (`StructuredTableTransformTest` 15/0/0: clean→exact GFM, ragged pad/overflow, pipe-escape, citations-survive, <2-col→list, low-confidence→list, no-fence identity, prose preserved, two-blocks, idempotence; + `ChatRepositoryTest` STRUCTURED-persists-a-table + FULL-byte-identical goldens). The reformat re-ask is deliberately **deferred to PA.5** (keeps the transform pure). Replaces PA.2's GFM-exemplar nudge for E2B STRUCTURED. Device adherence (does Gemma emit the `TABLE::` format reliably) → `VERIFICATION.md` K11 `[E]`-pending. **Watch-items:** #1662; fine-tune (FunctionGemma 58%→85%) as the model-side lever if ever needed. **Rejected:** a 2nd runtime, a JNI LLGuidance shim.
- **PA.5 — collection-scale pannable knowledge-map (the P-Atlas apex).** Replaces PA.1's static, phone-cramped Mermaid star with a **pannable/zoomable** map at collection scale, plus a "view as map" on the per-paper Connections section. **Design C (layout-as-data)** won an Ultracode judge-panel (3 designs × 3 adversarial lenses; C placed first-or-tied on all three): the *entire* layout + clustering + level-of-detail is computed **deterministically in pure `:core:search`** and emitted as a serializable `GraphScene` the renderer only blits + pans — so legibility is a JVM golden, not a device gamble; **zero new deps/assets, no JS, no telemetry, renders in airplane mode** (same red-line cleanliness as PA.1). User-approved forks: a **full-screen nav destination** (a canvas can't share the Ask sheet's vertical scroll), **augment** (not replace) the Connections list with "View as map", **hard cap ~400 nodes** by centrality. PA.1's per-paper Mermaid star is **kept** as the verified single-paper/airplane static fallback (one shared relation-sourcing core, two intentional render paths). Split into 3 PRs — pure `:core` first, so legibility is locked before any UI exists:
  - [x] **PA.5a — `:core:search` layout engine + scene (no UI; fully golden-tested off-device).** A pure `GraphLayoutEngine.layout(RelationGraph): GraphScene` — deterministic **Fruchterman–Reingold** per connected component (Vogel-sunflower init keyed on *sorted rank*, never RNG/list-index; nodes+edges **canonicalised** so output is invariant to input order; only IEEE-deterministic math + `StrictMath.{sin,cos,sqrt}` so Linux CI == Windows dev to the bit; coords rounded 2dp), with disconnected components **shelf-packed** so they can never overlap (plain FR drifts unboundedly on a disconnected graph). `GraphScene`/`SceneNode`/`SceneEdge`/`SceneBounds` are `@Serializable` (kotlinx-serialization added to `:core:search`; `RelationEdgeKind` annotated). **Naïve O(n²) repulsion, no Barnes–Hut** — the ~400 cap bounds it; the quadtree is a deferred optimisation, not correctness. Tests (`GraphLayoutEngineTest` 12/0/0, pure JVM): determinism (twice → identical), **order-invariance** (reversed input → identical scene), disconnected-box non-overlap, 50-node legibility (min pairwise ≥10, real 2D extent — the anti-node-soup proof, structural not brittle-exact-bytes), + edge cases (empty/single/dup-id/self-loop/unknown-endpoint/reverse-dup-dedup/degree/rounded-weight). No device surface.
  - [x] **PA.5b — clustering + level-of-detail tiers (still `:core`).** `GraphClusterer` uses **deterministic Louvain modularity local-moving** (a blueprint deviation — plain label-propagation with a deterministic min-label tie-break *floods across any bridge* and collapses a connected collection into one blob ≈ connected-components, making inter-cluster meta-edges dead; modularity correctly *subdivides* a connected mass, so a single citation bridge between two dense topics stays two clusters), with a **`primary_category` fallback** when there are no edges and cluster label = the highest-degree member's title. `GraphSceneBuilder` does **prune → layout → cluster**: pruning keeps all citations + each node's top-`SIMILAR_K=4` above-`SIMILARITY_FLOOR=0.3` similarity links (either-endpoint k-NN) so it can't go O(n²)-dense. The baked LoD ladder on `GraphScene` (`visibleAt(tier)`/`hitTest`, all `@Serializable`): **overview** = one super-node per real cluster (size ≥ 2) + a single **"Unconnected (N)"** holding node, capped at `OVERVIEW_MAX=12` (top 11 by size + the bucket), inter-group edges bundled into one weighted meta-edge per pair → **mid** (every paper, top-degree labelled) → **detail** (every paper labelled, all edges). Tests (`GraphSceneBuilderTest` 5, `GraphClustererTest` 6, `GraphSceneLodTest` 6 — all pure JVM): prune (cites-kept / floor / mutual-weakest k-NN / degree-1-leaf-kept), build determinism + order-invariance, community detection (2 cliques, star→1, singleton→−1, category fallback, highest-degree label), overview ≤12 on a 300-node fixture, unconnected bucket count, meta-edge bundling, mid-vs-detail labelling, hit-test (paper/cluster/empty). No device surface — the artifact is fully verified off-device here.
  - [x] **PA.5c — collection-graph data layer (`:app` repo + `:core:database` query; no UI, fully unit-tested).** Split out of the original combined PR (the device-bound Canvas is the risk; isolating the testable data layer keeps it off-device-verifiable). A read-only `LibraryDao.paperIdsForCollection(collectionId): List<String>` (no migration — `collection_papers` already exists) + a `CollectionGraphRepository`/`CollectionGraphSource` fun-interface mirroring `RelationGraphRepository`: member ids → citation edges (`CitationDao.edgesAmong`) ⊕ in-collection-filtered similarity (`EmbeddingDao.neighborsFor`) → **hard cap to the `MAX_NODES=400` most-central papers** (incident-edge degree, ties by id) → `GraphSceneBuilder.build` → `CollectionGraphResult.{Ready(scene), NoPapers, NoRelations}`. Hilt-bound in `AppModule`. **No repository cache** — the ViewModel survives config-change (holds the scene in its `StateFlow`), so rotation never re-derives and nothing is parcelled (dodges the Binder limit); a cache is a later optimisation if a cold open ever feels slow. Tests: `LibraryDaoTest` (paperIdsForCollection, Robolectric) + `CollectionGraphRepositoryTest` (Robolectric real-DB: NoPapers / NoRelations / Ready / non-member-edge-ignored) + a pure `capByCentrality` unit test. Full `./gradlew build` green. No device surface.
  - [x] **PA.5d — thin Compose Canvas renderer + wiring (`:app`; the only device-bound PR, the spike).** `KnowledgeMapViewModel` (Hilt, `SavedStateHandle` scope+id → `Loading|Ready(GraphScene)|Empty`; reuses `CollectionGraphSource` for collection scope and `RelationGraphSource`→`GraphSceneBuilder.build` for paper scope) + `KnowledgeMapScreen` + `KnowledgeMapCanvas` (blit + `detectTransformGestures` pan/zoom + tap `hitTest`, tier-by-zoom via `visibleAt`; the projection/fit/tier maths extracted to a pure `MapViewport`/`computeViewport`/`tierForZoom` so the fiddly screen↔layout maths are golden-tested off-device) + a mandatory **"View as list"** Compose a11y/low-end fallback (cluster-grouped + an "Unconnected (N)" section), a full-screen `map/{scope}/{id}` nav destination, both entry points (collection `TopAppBar` "Knowledge map" + Connections "View as map" — both `Icons.Filled.Hub`), empty/loading/error states, light/dark previews, strings. **Reuses the same `GraphSceneBuilder` pipeline for both scopes**, so PA.1's per-paper relation graph also gets the pannable canvas. Tests: `KnowledgeMapViewportTest` (projection round-trip, **focal-zoom invariance**, focus-on-point centring, fit, tier thresholds) + `KnowledgeMapViewModelTest` (collection Ready/Empty + paper-scope build, via the fun-interface sources as fakes). **Pre-merge adversarial review (Ultracode, 4 dims × adversarial verify): 10/11 confirmed findings folded in** — 2 majors (focal-anchored pinch-zoom so the graph grows under the fingers, not about the bounds-centre; a **cluster/holding super-node tap now drills in** — `focusOn` zooms+centres so members surface, since the overview tier has no tappable paper) + minors/nits (pan/zoom now `rememberSaveable` so rotation keeps the viewport; hoisted `PathEffect`; edge viewport-culling; section-header `maxLines`/ellipsis; toggle `stateDescription` for TalkBack; an Empty-state "Try again" wired to `load()`; the paper-scope empty strings moved to dedicated `knowledge_map_*` so the screen stops borrowing Ask's copy). The 1 dismissed finding (unguarded `id.toLong()`) was correctly ruled unreachable. Full `./gradlew build` green (Android lint clean). Device checks → `VERIFICATION.md` **K12** (collection map pans/zooms/clusters legibly **offline** at N≈50/150; rotate-survives; theme recolor) + **K13** (per-paper "View as map" + TalkBack reads "View as list").
- [x] **CHECKPOINT P-Atlas:** CI green per PR; the relation graph renders on every tier incl. none + airplane mode with valid Mermaid + designed empty states; redaction goldens green; richness ladder cloud-FULL byte-identical; PA.0 findings recorded; device checks in `VERIFICATION.md`. **Verified 2026-06-26:** every subphase merged green (PA.1 keystone · PA.0 spike · PA.2 richness ladder · PA.3a/3b light tier · PA.4 app-draws-the-structure tables · PA.5a/5b/5c/5d knowledge map — PRs #44–#61, each `Build, test, lint` green before self-merge); the full `./gradlew build` is green on the merged `main` (compile + all unit tests + ktlint + Android lint across every module). **Red lines hold:** the relation graph + collection knowledge map are **app-drawn from local data** (no provider/network/rate-limiter on the render path; render in airplane mode), so the redaction goldens (`ChatPreviewBuilderTest`/`PayloadBuilderTest`) and the cloud-FULL byte-identity goldens (`ChatContextAssemblerTest`/`ChatRepositoryTest`) are untouched and green; `:core:*` never depends on `:app`. **PA.0 findings recorded** (ROADMAP decision log + `.claude/memory/`). **Device-observable checks tracked in `VERIFICATION.md`:** K9 (Gemma STRUCTURED tables) + K10 (Qwen light tier) are `[E]`-verified; K11 (Gemma `TABLE::` adherence), K12 (collection map pans/zooms/clusters offline), K13 (per-paper "View as map" + TalkBack "View as list") are `[ ]`-pending an emulator session (device-only verification never blocks `[x]` on a green build — it's tracked, not assumed).
- [x] **PA.6 — hotfix: on-device readiness single-source (user device report 2026-07-03).** A Qwen-only device (the light tier's entire 3–4 GB target segment) got `ask_not_configured`: `AppModule`'s `onDeviceReady` seam hand-enumerated `gemma||nano` (written in P2.2 when exactly those two engines existed) and went stale when PA.3a grew the engine list. Fix = **structural**, not a one-liner: `OnDeviceProvider.isReady()` (any wired engine) is now the single readiness source and the resolver seam delegates to it — resolution can never again disagree with `chat()`. + `EngineCachePreflight` (a full disk made the native XNNPack cache write **SIGABRT the whole app** on first engine init — reproduced live at 88% disk; now a graceful `AppError.Storage`). + regression pins (`AppModuleResolverWiringTest` executes the real `@Provides` composition Qwen-only; `ResolverReadinessSourceStructuralTest` makes hand-enumeration a red build; true-side `isReady` pins for both engines) + the stale-copy sweep (the settings screen literally said on-device "arrives in a later update"). Emulator-verified (K20): pre-fix repro → post-fix on-device resolution, same device state. Docs/spec synced (SPEC-AI-PROVIDERS §3/§5/§6a/§6b/§7/§8, CLAUDE.md hosts red line, on-device-ai.md). *(A new shape: the first post-checkpoint hotfix row in a closed phase — recorded here so the phase's ledger stays complete.)*

## Phase P-Share — "export, share, and act on everything" (v2-era, user-directed 2026-06-26)

> Reshapes + expands the three deferred P-Rich follow-ons (R2.5 svg · R4.2 export · R4-TTS) into a cohesive **export / share / act** surface. **Thesis:** every artifact the app produces — an answer, a diagram, the knowledge map, the paper itself, its citations — is one tap from **copy / share / save / export / speak**, via consistent **per-bubble contextual actions** on both user and assistant bubbles. Planned via an Ultracode workflow (4 surface maps → 6 designs → a judge-panel on the R4.2 capture fork → synthesis); the panel **web-verified the decisive fact** that `createPrintDocumentAdapter` fires on `onPageFinished` (HTML *loaded*, not async-JS *rendered*) — so the old "prefer print-adapter→PDF" steer was wrong, and image export uses a **signaled off-screen WebView → PNG** capture instead. User-directed scope: world-class breadth + **jsoup adopted** (raw-svg rendered safely now; positions the **ar5iv/HTML paper-reading vision**, promoted out of the do-not-work backlog). Red lines hold: user-initiated, OS-share-sheet/clipboard only, **no upload**, AI key never involved, offline/airplane-safe, no telemetry, `:core:*` ∌ `:app`, chat never routed through the importable backup schema. Sequence: smallest/security-first → the real capture spike last.

- [x] **PS.1 — raw-`svg` rendering, jsoup-sanitized (was R2.5).** Adopted **jsoup** (the project's first HTML/XML-parse dep — a vetted parser for a security-critical surface; also the future ar5iv/HTML engine). Raw ` ```svg ` is now a **rendered** block (not the inert code box): a pure `:core:ai` **`SvgSanitizer`** — jsoup **XML**-parse (not HTML — preserves SVG camelCase + namespaces) + an **element-allowlist parse-and-rebuild** (keep `svg/g/path/rect/circle/ellipse/line/poly*/text/tspan/defs/lineargradient/radialgradient/stop/clipPath/mask/pattern/use/style/marker/symbol`; drop `script`/`foreignObject`/`image`/`a`/`animate*` + their subtree) with a **dangerous-attribute denylist** (all `on*`; `href`/`xlink:href`/`src` unless `#frag`/inline `data:image`; any `javascript:`/`expression(`/`@import`/external `url()` value; `<style>` body emptied when dangerous). `RichHtml` HTML-unescapes commonmark's escaped fence → `SvgSanitizer.sanitize` → inline `<div class="svg">` vector on the sandboxed WebView (null → the inert code box; the rendered span is added to `PROTECTED` so citation linkification can't claw into `<path d="…[0]…">`). Tests: `SvgSanitizerTest` 14/0/0 (adversarial corpus: script/case-obfuscated/foreignObject/handlers/external-refs/js-href/dangerous-style → neutralised shape-only; benign + local-frag refs + camelCase + inline style → preserved; no-svg/oversized → null) + `RichHtmlTest` ×5 (gate routes svg; pipeline renders sanitized / neutralises malicious / falls back on non-svg / skips citations). The svg caption "Image." is pre-seeded for PS.2. Device render → `VERIFICATION.md` K14.
- [x] **PS.2 — read-aloud (R4-TTS).** Pure `SpeakableText` extractor (`:app`, JVM-golden — `mermaid`→"Diagram", `$$…$$`/` ```math `→"Equation", ` ```svg `→"Image", reads a trivial inline `$x$` but captions complex math, drops `[n]`, speaks `arXiv:id` without the colon, strips markdown/links/lists/tables/fences, **never** reads LaTeX or the Sources block — the Sources live in `message.citations`, not `text`) + a `@Singleton TextToSpeechManager` behind a narrow **`ReadAloud`** seam (so `AskViewModel` stays unit-testable): lazy async init, `Locale.getDefault()`→`ENGLISH`→graceful-disable, `UtteranceProgressListener` drives a `speakingId` StateFlow, sentence-chunked under `getMaxSpeechInputLength()`, never crashes. The **Read-aloud** action is wired **inside `AskSheet`** (so all three Ask hosts get it for free) as a per-answer play/stop `TextButton`, keyed by answer content; stops on sheet-dismiss + app-background via `LocalLifecycleOwner` `ON_STOP` (no `lifecycle-process` dep — it isn't catalogued, and the plan's fallback is honoured) + the VM's `onCleared`. Builds the exact `TextToSpeechManager` P3 "read the paper aloud" reuses. Tests: `SpeakableTextTest` 9/0/0 (per-block captions + markdown strip + the no-machine-syntax invariant) + `TextToSpeechManagerTest` 3/0/0 (pure chunker) + `AskViewModelTest` updated for the `ReadAloud` seam. Device playback → `VERIFICATION.md` K15.
- [x] **PS.3 — per-bubble contextual-actions framework.** A reusable `BubbleActions` surface on **both** user and assistant bubbles (user-approved pattern: a **compact inline icon row + an overflow ⋮ menu**, the ChatGPT/Claude norm — discoverable yet uncluttered, scales as PS.4/5 add actions). Assistant bubbles: inline **Copy** (the markdown answer, via `LocalClipboardManager` — `message.text` is already markdown, so this *is* "copy as markdown") · **Read aloud** (PS.2, relocated) · **Share** (R4, relocated), with an overflow housing **Pin to notes** (R3a, relocated, paper-scope) · **Quote in a follow-up** (new — prepends a capped blockquote of the answer into the Ask input via `setInput`). **User questions** — which had **zero** actions — gain a lone **Copy**. Wired **inside `AskSheet`** (so all three Ask hosts inherit it), each callback null-hides its action; replaces the old three-`TextButton` row. **Export-as-image hooks in at PS.4; BibTeX/save-to-notes round out at PS.5.** **Long-press deferred** (would fight in-bubble citation/link taps + the rich WebView — the inline+overflow fully delivers the discoverable set). Compile + Android-lint green (UI-only; the per-bubble surface is device-verified). Device check → `VERIFICATION.md` K16.
- **PS.4 — image export (R4.2, reshaped to PNG).** Split into a tested foundation + the device-bound capture (the plan's "land the flaky render-signal seam tested before any device code").
  - [x] **PS.4a — FileProvider + share helper + capture geometry (foundation, off-device-tested).** A `FileProvider` (`${applicationId}.fileprovider` + `res/xml/file_paths.xml` → `cache-path` `ask_exports/` only; distinct from `.androidx-startup`) + `Context.shareImage(file, subject)` (ACTION_SEND, `image/png`, EXTRA_STREAM, per-share read grant). Originally also shipped a JS render-signal (`RichHtml.answerHtml(forCapture=true)` firing `arxiver://rendered`) — **superseded in PS.4b**: device verification (K17) proved an off-screen WebView ticks no frames, so the rAF-wrapped signal never fires; PS.4b drives capture from the host instead and the `forCapture` script + `RichRenderSignal.heightPx` were removed (`RichRenderSignal.deviceHeightPx` kept). (FileProvider config device-verified at PS.4b — the Robolectric round-trip is a Windows `getCanonicalPath` flake, not a config bug.)
  - [x] **PS.4b — off-screen capture + wire (device-verified, K17).** Extracted `WebView.applyRichSandbox()` + a shared `RichTheme`/`rememberRichTheme` (on-screen + capture render identically, and the capture can't drift from `blockNetworkLoads=true`). `RichImageExporter`: attaches a capture WebView (occluded by the modal sheet, `alpha=0.004` — **non-zero so the compositor keeps producing frames**, else the async Mermaid/fonts render is starved), the **host owns timing** (coroutine `delay` + host-initiated `evaluateJavascript` polling for fonts+Mermaid-`<svg>` readiness, immune to the renderer's off-screen page-timer throttling), measures the **max element bottom** (a Mermaid `<svg>` overflows its body box → `getBoundingClientRect().height` clips the last node), software-layer `draw()` → opaque PNG in `cache/ask_exports/` → `shareImage` (now sets **`ClipData`** so the chooser preview gets the read grant). Wired **Export as image** into the PS.3 per-bubble overflow (rich answers only, `RichContent.has`). **Three device-found bugs fixed** (off-screen rAF/timer starvation → host-driven; svg-overflow height clip; chooser-preview FileProvider grant) — see `VERIFICATION.md` K17 + log. The **native knowledge-map PNG** (re-render the scene at fit-all bounds) + a PDF-for-tall-answers path remain documented fast-follows.
- [x] **PS.5 — save/share the paper + citations.** A paper-detail bar **overflow ⋮** (beside the existing one-tap Share) housing **Share PDF · Copy reference · Copy BibTeX**. **Share PDF** shares the already-downloaded `filesDir/pdfs/<id>v*.pdf` (resolved via a new single-source **`PdfStorage`** util — also de-dups the path convention out of `PdfPageImageSource`/`PdfViewerViewModel`/`SettingsViewModel`) through the **scoped** FileProvider (`file_paths.xml` gains a `files-path pdfs/`; `Context.sharePdf` mirrors `shareImage`/`shareText`, `application/pdf` + `ClipData` preview grant); when the PDF isn't on device it **falls back to sharing the arXiv PDF link** (text, **no** on-demand download → the arXiv rate limiter is never touched on a share). **Copy reference / Copy BibTeX** put a one-line formatted reference / a BibTeX `@misc{…}` on the clipboard — both from a **pure `:core:model` `Citation`** generator (token-free, all metadata local; `CitationTest` 8/0/0). **Already satisfied by earlier subphases (verified, not rebuilt):** *Share arXiv link* = the existing detail Share button (title + abs URL); *Save an answer to Notes* = PS.3's **Pin to notes** (`onPinAnswer → addNote`). **Scope correction (self-healed):** the plan's "a formatted reference for the paper *and* its cited sources … all metadata already on-device" was **wrong for cited sources** — a paper's references are stored only as `s2_stub` rows (title + arXiv id; no authors/year/doi — SPEC-DATA §2), so a researcher-grade cited-source reference isn't derivable on-device; cited-source export is **deferred** until `CitationSyncWorker` enriches author/year. The focused paper's own citation *is* researcher-grade (its metadata is complete locally). Device check → `VERIFICATION.md` K18.
- [x] **PS.6 — whole-conversation export.** The Ask sheet's header share icon now opens an export menu with **Share as text · Export Markdown file · Export as PDF** (replacing the single text-share). All three are owned **inside `AskSheet`** (like the PS.4b PNG export) — the host only supplies a display `conversationTitle` (the old `onShareConversation` host closures across PaperDetail / ChatHistory / FilteredPapers collapse to one value param). **Share as text** = `ConversationMarkdown.conversation` → OS sheet (the prior behavior, kept). **Markdown file** writes that same Markdown to `cache/ask_exports/conversation_*.md` and shares it via the PS.4 FileProvider (`text/markdown`, new generic `Context.shareFile`). **PDF** = a new `ConversationPdfPrinter`: renders the conversation Markdown → the chat's rich HTML (`RichHtml`) on a fixed **light/print** theme → the **system print pipeline** (`WebView.createPrintDocumentAdapter` + `PrintManager`) for **native multi-page pagination** (the thing PNG couldn't do for a tall conversation), reusing PS.4b's host-driven WebView-readiness wait so KaTeX/Mermaid finish before print; the WebView is kept alive until the print job finishes, then destroyed. Red lines hold: chat is serialized only through `ConversationMarkdown` (never the backup schema), user-initiated, offline, no upload, key untouched. Pure content stays golden-tested (`ConversationMarkdownTest`, `RichHtmlTest`); the file-share + print surface is device-bound → `VERIFICATION.md` K19.
- [x] **CHECKPOINT P-Share:** CI green per PR (PS.1–PS.6, each `Build, test, lint` green before self-merge — latest PS.6 #71); full `./gradlew build` green on merged `main`. **Red lines verified 2026-06-26** (an adversarial 6-line audit — one agent per red line, each hunting for a violation — plus a deterministic grep + the build gate): export/share/copy/read-aloud/print are **user-initiated + OS-sheet/clipboard/system-print only** — the share helpers (`ShareText`/`ShareImage`/`SharePdf`/`ShareFile`, `RichImageExporter`, `ConversationPdfPrinter`) contain **no network primitive** (ACTION_SEND/FileProvider/PrintManager/clipboard only); the render WebViews set `blockNetworkLoads=true` + load only bundled `file:///android_asset` KaTeX/Mermaid (**offline/airplane-safe**); the **AI key is never read** on any export path; **chat is serialized only through `ConversationMarkdown`** — `BackupManager`/`LibraryExporter` reference no chat table (**backup-wall** intact; `ChatPreviewBuilderTest`/`PayloadBuilderTest`/`BackupManagerTest` green); `:core:*` ∌ `:app` (incl. the new pure `:core:model` `Citation`). **Shipped:** PS.1 svg+jsoup · PS.2 read-aloud · PS.3 per-bubble actions · PS.4a/4b PNG export · PS.5 paper/citation save+share · PS.6 conversation export (text/Markdown-file/PDF). **Device checks in `VERIFICATION.md`:** K14/K15/K16/K17 `[E]`-verified; K11 `[~]`, K18 (PS.5) + K19 (PS.6) `[ ]`-pending an emulator session (device-only verification never blocks `[x]` on a green build — tracked, not assumed).

**Folded-in wins (this phase):** K11 Gemma `TABLE::` device check · harden flaky `PaperDetailViewModelTest` (inject the test dispatcher) · K12 adaptive cluster-drill (fit-to-cluster zoom, replaces the fixed 2.6×) · K7 collection-Ask label ("Chat with this collection").

**Captured vision (promoted out of the do-not-work backlog):** **P-HTML / ar5iv** — render the arXiv **HTML** edition of a paper for a richer reading experience; **jsoup** (adopted in PS.1) is the parsing engine. **Now an active phase** (planned 2026-06-27 via two Ultracode passes) — see **Phase P-HTML** below.

## Phase P-HTML — render the arXiv HTML edition (ar5iv) + elevate the reading surface (v2-era, user-directed 2026-06-27)

> Turn the reading surface from **PDF + abstract** into a **reflowable, math-native, link-rich, airplane-safe** HTML reader (native `arxiv.org/html/<id>` primary → `ar5iv.labs.arxiv.org` fallback → existing PDF as the never-strand floor), plus a deliberate UX elevation of the paper-reading surface. **jsoup** (adopted PS.1) parses + sanitizes the untrusted LaTeXML document in `:core:ai`; fetch/hosts/storage in `:core:network`; reader screen/VM in `:app`. Planned via an Ultracode map+research pass (native HTML is live for 2026 papers; both sources emit LaTeXML 0.8.8 + real MathML; CDN refs `use.typekit.net`/`cdn.jsdelivr.net` must be stripped; robots allows `/html`) → a design pass (3 stances → a 6-agent adversarial judge panel × 3 lenses → synthesis) that caught 4 execution ship-blockers (parser-differential mXSS → CSP + fixed-point; broken `file://` images → virtual-origin; suspend-vs-sync OkHttp interceptor coupling the AI-key client → dedicated client; cache-completeness/back-stack). Governed by **`docs/SPEC-P-HTML.md`**. Red lines hold: sanitize-before-WebView, offline/airplane-safe (`blockNetworkLoads=true`, bundled assets), no upload/telemetry, key off the render/fetch path, every fetch through the ≥3s arXiv limiter, `:core:* ∌ :app`, rendered HTML off the importable backup schema. **Verified gaps this phase closes:** the PDF fetch currently **bypasses** the ≥3s limiter, and **no `AllowedHosts`** exists. **Locked forks:** F1 strip images in MVP → virtual-origin pre-fetch PH.5 · F2 allowlist `HtmlSanitizer` + CSP + fixed-point + shared cleaner + MathML surface · F3 separate route + additive "Read HTML" button · F4 native MathML + runtime fallback · F5 dedicated rate-limited client + suspend-at-seam + per-hop host reject + PDF-bypass fix · F6 filesystem-only cache + DTO/OS-backup posture + `.complete`. MVP cut = PH.0→PH.4; elevation = PH.5–PH.8.

- [x] **PH.0 — SPEC-P-HTML + threat model + committed adversarial corpus (docs + test resources only).** Wrote `docs/SPEC-P-HTML.md` (source decision + canonical-versioned-URL resolution, LaTeXML markup contract for native + ar5iv, conversion-fidelity markers, the `HtmlSanitizer` threat model incl. CSP + fixed-point + MathML annotation-xml/maction/href + `<svg>` delegation + caps + off-main, the AllowedHosts + dedicated-client + suspend-at-seam + per-hop-reject rate-limit contract, image-delivery (virtual-origin/`data:`, never bare `file://`), filesystem-only storage + `.complete` + DTO/OS-backup posture, nav/fallback UX, the F1–F6 locked positions, MVP cut). Committed the corpus under `core/ai/src/test/resources/phtml/`: **real** trimmed excerpts — `native-clean-2412.19437` (resolvable bib, absolute cite hrefs, jsdelivr), `native-degraded-2510.04905` (419 `ltx_missing_citation`, zero bib, native MathML `intent=`, Typekit, `onclick`), `ar5iv-clean-1706.03762` (bare-fragment cites, ar5iv markup) + a hand-built `malicious-battery.html` (every §5 vector) + `PROVENANCE.md`. No production code. Green build.
- [x] **PH.1 — `HtmlSanitizer` in `:core:ai` + shared-cleaner refactor + adversarial golden corpus.** Extracted `SvgSanitizer`'s allowlist cleaner into a shared internal `SanitizerCore` (parameterised `Ruleset` + `clean(Element, depth, rs, budget)`); refactored `SvgSanitizer` onto it (its 14 tests stay byte-identical). New `HtmlSanitizer` (jsoup `htmlParser`, `HTML_RULESET` = HTML body + full MathML allowlist; drops all `on*`/`script`/`style`/`link`/`base`/`meta`/`iframe`/`object`/`embed`/`form`/`button`/`foreignObject` + MathML `maction`/`annotation-xml`; **per-attr URI policy** — auto-loading `src` strict to local/`data:image`/same-origin-relative, navigational `href` kept-unless-dangerous-scheme so the transform can internalise it; raised `MAX_INPUT`=6 MB + 250k node-count cap; emits sanitized `<body>` only, deterministic compact output, null-on-reject; caller runs it off-main under `withTimeout`). Tests: `HtmlSanitizerTest` 12/0/0 — the malicious battery → **structurally inert** (re-parse + element inspect, so escaped text can't false-positive) with benign LaTeXML/MathML/camelCase-svg surviving; the 3 real fixtures benign-survive + stay inert; `sanitize(x)==sanitize(sanitize(x))` fixed-point holds across the corpus; + focused inline cases. `SvgSanitizerTest` 14/0/0 unchanged. Full `./gradlew build` green. SPEC-P-HTML §5 refined (src-vs-href URI split; `annotation-xml` dropped wholesale) in the same commit.
- [x] **PH.2 — `AllowedHosts` + dedicated rate-limited client + PDF bypass fix (own PR, before HTML feature code).** `AllowedHosts` {export.arxiv.org, arxiv.org, ar5iv.labs.arxiv.org, api.semanticscholar.org, huggingface.co} + `AllowedHostsInterceptor` (pure-sync; rejects non-https/non-allowlisted with `IOException`→`AppError.Offline`) in `:core:network`. An `@ArxivClient`-qualified dedicated `OkHttpClient` (via `okHttpClient.newBuilder()`) carries the gate as **both** an application interceptor (disallowed *original* host → no socket) **and** a network interceptor (per redirect hop — Fastly 3xx). `arxivApiClient` + `pdfDownloader` switch to `@ArxivClient`; AI providers/routine/model-downloaders stay bare (key path uncoupled, asserted). **`PdfDownloader` retrofitted** — takes the limiter, `acquire()` only **after** the cache-hit short-circuit + a descriptive User-Agent → the verified ≥3s bypass is closed. **No host-keying** (single global limiter spaces the whole arXiv group; host-keying would break `ArxivRateLimiter`/`ArxivApiClient` tests for no red-line gain); **S2's 1.2 s mutex = sole documented exception** (stays bare). `ArxivRateLimiter` made `open` for a counting test double. Tests: `AllowedHostsTest` (5), `AllowedHostsInterceptorTest` (5 — allow via fake `Chain`, http/disallowed reject, pre-connection no-socket, AI-client uncoupling), `PdfDownloaderTest` (3 — cache-hit zero-acquire/zero-request, cache-miss acquire-once, error mapping), `NoDirectNewCallStructuralTest` (1 — guards future fetchers); existing `ArxivApiClientTest`/`ArxivRateLimiterTest` unchanged-green. Fixed a `:app` `PdfViewerViewModelTest` for the new ctor. Full `./gradlew build` green (after the known `FilteredPapersViewModelTest` flake cleared on re-run). SPEC §7 reworded (no host-keying; S2 exception; `huggingface.co` resolved) + VERIFICATION §M1 added in the same commit. Device check → `VERIFICATION.md` **M1**.
- [x] **PH.3 — `HtmlFetcher` + `HtmlStorage` + LaTeXML→reader transform + reader CSS (pure + fetch, no UI).** Planned via an Ultracode pass (5 mappers → blueprint → 3-lens stress) **+ a personal adversarial validation** ([[personal-adversarial-plan-validation]]) that corrected the plan (dropped a redundant `dataExtractionRules` edit — root `.` is already excluded; dropped the self-size script + the dead `:app` CSS asset) and augmented it (boundary-anchored id match; bib-targeting fidelity; `.complete` carries the source). Tests: `HtmlReaderTransformTest` (16 — real fixtures + dual-cite/boundary/external/fidelity/img/body-fallback), `ReaderDocWriterTest` (2), `HtmlFetcherTest` (5 — MockWebServer + host-rewrite + counting limiter: native-OK/404-bare/degraded→ar5iv/all-404→PDF/offline), `HtmlStorageTest` (3), `HtmlFetcherNoBypassStructuralTest` (AI-provider-excepted). `:core:ai` 140 tests green; full `./gradlew build` green. - [x] **PH.5 — offline figure pre-fetch + `data:`-inline delivery (elevation).** Planned via an Ultracode pass (3 mappers incl. live arXiv/ar5iv research → 3 design stances → a 3-lens adversarial judge panel → high-effort synthesis) **+ a personal adversarial validation** ([[personal-adversarial-plan-validation]]) that **endorsed the surprising winner** (`data:`-inline over the SPEC's reserved virtual origin — an https virtual origin is suppressed by `blockNetworkImage=true`, forcing it off; `data:` keeps **both** network blocks armed with `baseUrl=null`, no new dep, no `shouldInterceptRequest`) and **caught 3 load-bearing bugs in the blueprint**: (1) the image-URL base must be the **exact fetched page URL** (`…/html/<id>v<ver>`, no trailing slash) — the blueprint's `…/<id>v<ver>/` base would **double** the version dir for native's version-prefixed srcs (confirmed against live arXiv); (2) the two-phase **re-store overwrites `index.html`**, which `File.renameTo` won't do on the Windows JVM test host → `HtmlStorage.store` switched to `Files.move(REPLACE_EXISTING)`; (3) `withTimeoutOrNull(fetchAll())` **discards partials** on timeout → the fetcher now **emits each image via a callback** so the deadline keeps figures fetched so far. Shipped: `ReaderImage`/`InlinedImage` + a (never-persisted) `images` manifest on `ReaderDocument`; `HtmlReaderTransform` rewrites relative same-origin `<img>` → opaque `data-img-key` token + manifest (resolved against the exact page URL, host-allowlisted, count-capped; `data:` srcs kept; over-cap/external → figcaption) + a cheap `assertNoExternalHost` cache re-gate; **`HtmlImageFetcher`** (`:core:ai`, mirrors `HtmlFetcher`'s `@ArxivClient`+`acquire()`; serial, cancellable, `Content-Type` raster allowlist, per-image + total byte caps, base64 via `java.util.Base64`); **`HtmlImageInliner`** (pure token→`data:` URI / placeholder); the ViewModel's **two-phase render** (placeholder body first → fetch+inline+re-store+re-expose, deadline-bounded); reader.css `img{max-width:100%}`; DI provider; `HtmlReaderWebView` stays `baseUrl=null` + both network blocks armed (KDoc corrected). Caps `IMAGE_COUNT_CAP=40` / `IMAGE_MAX_BYTES=600 KB` / `IMAGE_TOTAL_BYTES_BUDGET=4 MB` (ctor-injectable) / `IMAGE_FETCH_DEADLINE_MS=30 s` — **PROVISIONAL, device-ratify** (HUMAN.md). Tests: `HtmlReaderTransformTest` (+native/ar5iv resolution, `data:`-kept, external-rejected, dedup, over-cap), `HtmlImageInlinerTest` (data: form + sanitizer fixed-point), `HtmlImageFetcherTest` (serial/acquire-count/non-2xx/oversize/budget/non-raster, MockWebServer), `HtmlStorageTest` (overwrite round-trip), `HtmlReaderViewModelTest` (two-phase inline + poisoned-cache re-gate), `ReaderDocWriterTest` (img css). `native-clean` fixture src corrected to the real version-prefixed form. Tests: `AskQuoteTest` (incl. blockquote-breakout + ellipsis-fix goldens), `ReaderScrollJsTest` selection set (U+2028/2029/NBSP collapse, bidi/zero-width strip, re-cap, garbage), `ReaderWebViewTest` (one-Ask-item idempotence, delegation, no-sync-finish, double-tap guard, sandbox-on-subclass), `ReaderScrollControllerTest` (find stamping, readSelection null-delivery, reveal-once-per-generation incl. failsafe), `ReaderFindBarTest` (reducer matrix), `AskViewModelTest` offerQuote cases, `ChatPreviewBuilderTest` confirm-fidelity golden. - [-] **PH.8 — [device-gated] conditional bundled-offline MathML fallback — CLOSED NO-GO (2026-07-04).** The gate it was waiting for resolved against it: the M5 device measurement (VERIFICATION log 2026-07-04) shows **native Chromium MathML renders the stress sample adequately** (true fractions, radicals, scripts, display + inline, on the Attention paper's native edition), and the floor argument dissolved on a platform fact — **System WebView is a Play-updated APK on every API-26+ device**, so a genuinely frozen pre-M109 WebView is a museum-piece cohort (no-GMS/sideload-only devices) that the never-strand PDF fallback already serves. A bundled math engine (MB of binary + its own adversarial corpus + maintenance) buys negligible reach. **Reopening conditions (recorded, not dropped):** evidence of a real user cohort on frozen WebViews, or a device report of broken math on an updated WebView. The riders (figure tap-to-zoom, wide-table scroll) move to the backlog.
- [x] **CHECKPOINT P-HTML** (gates after PH.4): green build ✓; **off-device security gate green** ✓ — PH.1 adversarial corpus + `sanitize(x)==sanitize(sanitize(x))` fixed-point; PH.3 zero-external-host transform golden + CSP `script-src 'none'`; PH.2 per-hop `AllowedHosts` reject, `NoDirectNewCall` structural guard, AI-client uncoupled, backup DTO/OS-backup exclusion; the PDF ≥3s bypass closed (`PdfDownloaderTest` regression). **Device gate recorded in `VERIFICATION.md §M` (M2–M8, doesn't block `[x]`):** native + ar5iv render end-to-end, airplane-mode no-egress, native-MathML stress verdict on API-34 + an API-26/27 old-WebView AVD, fallback-to-PDF + back-stack, cross-ref/external-link confirm, TalkBack. SPEC-P-HTML current ✓. **MVP cut PH.0→PH.4 complete; elevation PH.5–PH.8 remain.**

## Phase P-Chat — chat becomes a first-class surface (v2-era, plan approved 2026-07-04)

> Promoted from the Future-phases capture. Thesis: the chat plumbing (persistent Room sessions, resume, collection KBs, selection→Ask) outgrew its placement — history is buried under Settings and conversations live in a cramped modal sheet. Planned via an Ultracode pass (3 mappers → 3 design stances → a 3-judge adversarial panel × architecture/data-safety/UX lenses → synthesis) **+ a personal adversarial validation** that verified every load-bearing claim at file:line — including the one bug all three stances missed until the judge pass: the **cross-surface session write-redirect** (`AskViewModel`'s unconditional post-turn re-sync to the scope's most-recent session — under two live hosts on one scope, surface A silently appends its next send to surface B's session). ~70% of the phase is promotion of shipped parts: `ChatHistoryScreen` already IS the recents surface, `AskSheet`'s only sheet coupling is one `ModalBottomSheet` line, and `ChatRepository` already supports forking (`stream()` lazily creates a session when `sessionId==null`). **Co-Founder amendment folded in (2026-07-04):** instead of a 5th bottom-bar tab, **Search + Browse merge into one "Explore" tab** (both are discovery: Search = dual-scope Library|arXiv query, Browse = remote taxonomy feed; local tags/collections live in Library) — end state a **4-tab bar: Today · Explore · Library · Chat** (PC.2 owns the merge as its own subphase with a focused planning pass). Ships: (0) hygiene + red-line hardening; (1) a full-screen conversation route via `ConversationHost` extraction + fork-new-session, deleting the ChatHistoryScreen VM-reuse bug structurally; (2) the Explore merge; (3) the Chat tab with a proper one-query recents surface (JOIN kills the N+1) + undo-delete; (4) ONE v3→v4 migration (pinned + nullable title + one-shot ghost sweep); (5) pinned sections + rename. Red lines held throughout: chat content NEVER enters `ArxiverBackup` (PC.0 makes this a failing descriptor test); one Room `Migration` + committed `4.json` + Robolectric test, destructive migration forbidden; redaction goldens untouched (no payload-path file is edited anywhere in the phase); strings.xml; TalkBack + light/dark previews; `:core:* ∌ :app`; no new hosts, no telemetry.

- [x] **PC.0 — chat hygiene + red-line hardening (no UI, no schema).** Shipped through an Ultracode adversarial review over the diff (2 lenses → 9 verify agents → 7 confirmed findings, ALL folded in — each strengthening a fix beyond the plan's form). (a) **Cross-surface write-redirect fix, exact-id form** (the kill-shot precondition for any second conversation host): the post-turn re-sync of `sessionId` to the scope's most-recent session is **deleted outright** — a first turn now binds via new `ChatRepository.ensureSession()` **before** streaming, adopting the EXACT id it creates. The review killed the plan's interim assign-only-when-null form: its "learn" still resolved *most-recent*, so two hosts starting first turns near-simultaneously could cross-bind on a timestamp race; pre-stream binding also closes the rapid-follow-up window after `streaming=false` publication. Turn entry points now also **join the hydration job**, so a send racing sheet-open can never snapshot a null binding and fork a phantom session. Regression test **proven to bite** (fix reverted → red → restored); a second test pins exact-id adoption against a planted newer foreign session. (b) **Ghost-bubble hygiene, both flavors**: hydration drops empty-INCOMPLETE assistant rows (the mid-stream-process-death artifact, seen live on device 2026-07-04) — non-empty partials and error rows survive, and the live streaming bubble renders from in-memory state so an active turn can never be hidden; AND the review-found empty-COMPLETE sibling is killed at the source — a provider `Done` with no usable text now persists as `error` (matching the error bubble the live UI already shows; an ''/complete row would dodge every ghost filter and feed an empty assistant turn into later model context). (c) **Backup-wall structural tests**: the exact top-level descriptor pin (`ArxiverBackup` = {schema, exportedAt, papers, follows, collections, routines}) PLUS a review-driven **recursive descriptor walk** over `ArxiverBackup` AND `LibraryExport` asserting no element at ANY depth is chat-shaped (chat/session/message/conversation) — a nested `chats` field on `ExportedPaper`/`BackupCollection` is now a red build, converting the red line from code-absence to test-enforced at full depth. Redaction goldens untouched.

## Phase P-Tools — agentic in-chat tool-use: the corpus becomes searchable mid-conversation (v2-era, plan approved 2026-07-04)

> Promoted from the Future-phases capture. Thesis: today retrieval is **RAG-before-the-turn** over what the user already holds; P-Tools gives the chat model a **local tool loop** (the Claude-connector model) so mid-conversation it can search the *living* corpus — the user's own library (**zero-egress, on-device**), arXiv, Semantic Scholar (arXiv+bioRxiv+medRxiv+PubMed+venues), and chemRxiv — reason over the results with the user's BYOK provider, and **import** papers straight into the P-HTML reader / PDF pipeline. Planned via an Ultracode pass (4 mappers → 3 design stances → a 3-lens adversarial judge panel [architecture · privacy-redline(veto) · scope-sequencing] → synthesis) **+ a personal adversarial validation** that verified every load-bearing claim at file:line on merged post-P-Chat code and **caught two under-specifications the plan missed**: (a) the `:core:ai` interface named only `toolResults` but omitted the **assistant-side `tool_use` representation** (`ChatMessage.toolCalls`) — Anthropic HTTP-400s on a `tool_result` without a matching `tool_use` in the preceding assistant turn, so the resume request must replay it; (b) the design's "suppress pre-turn RAG when tools on" collides with the `[n]` citation contract built from `assembled.citedChunks` (`ChatRepository.kt:155`) → deferred to a PT.1 decision, PT.0 leaves RAG untouched. Governed by **`docs/SPEC-P-TOOLS.md`**. **Chosen architecture — the loop lives ABOVE the provider:** a repo-driven `ChatToolLoop` in `ChatRepository.stream` (the sole owner of persistence + the `NonCancellable` finalize + the limiter/AllowedHosts seam + the disclosure surface); providers stay single-shot and gain three additive, **default-off** fields (`ChatRequest.tools`, `ChatChunk.ToolUse(id+name)`, a `ChatRole.TOOL` result turn + `ChatMessage.toolCalls`/`toolResults`) plus a `ProviderCapability.supportsTools` flag — so on-device **degrades cleanly to no-tools** and both redaction goldens stay byte-identical until a tool attaches. Loop-inside-the-provider (Stance B) was rejected: it can't reconstruct the in-flight message list after process death and splits disclosure across the module boundary — we harvested its SSE/migration/consent detail wholesale and only flipped the loop's location. Red lines held: every external fetch routes through the existing `AllowedHosts` + `@ArxivClient` ≥3s `ArxivRateLimiter` / S2 1.2s mutex / chemRxiv polite mutex (**no bypass**); a `MAX_TOOL_ITERATIONS=5` cap bounds cost (cap-hit → one final `tools`-omitted round, never a dangling `tool_use`); tool results are **public source data, not chat content**, but they **do** egress and are disclosed twice — the confirm lists tool *definitions*, the persistent inline activity log shows each model-minted query + source + `egress` flag; `tool_invocations` rides a new table FK'd to the assistant message (**not** new chat_messages roles) behind the six-field `ArxiverBackup` allowlist DTO + an **extended forbidden-name walk** (`tool/invocation/query/activity`); the optional S2 BYOK key lives only in `EncryptedSharedPreferences` via `AiKeyVault`; `:core:* ∌ :app`; no telemetry. **Sequenced to de-risk by egress:** PT.0 lands the loop + consent/disclosure + `MIGRATION_4_5` with a **fake local tool (zero egress)**; PT.1 proves the architecture with `search_my_library` (**still zero egress**); only **PT.2** opens the first external byte.

- [x] **PT.0 — tool-loop plumbing + consent/disclosure model (NO external tools).** Planned via an Ultracode pass (4 mappers → 2 blueprints → 3 adversarial judges [loop-correctness · red-line-veto · scope] → synthesis; 14 must-fixes folded) **+ a personal adversarial validation** ([[personal-adversarial-plan-validation]]) that verified every load-bearing claim at file:line and **cut two over-builds + fixed one implementation bug the plan carried**: (i) **the `core/claude PayloadBuilder` edit is spurious** — that's the SPEC-CLAUDE-BRIDGE **Routines** dispatch envelope (an outbound trigger, `RoutineAction`/papers/relations), wholly unrelated to chat tool-use; adding an always-null `tools` field would only pollute the `arxiver/v1` routines schema → **cut it**, so `PayloadBuilderTest` stays green *unedited* (SPEC §9 corrected in the same commit); (ii) a visible **consent toggle gates nothing in PT.0** (only a local, consent-free echo tool exists) → the `tools_enabled` migration column + repo seams ship, but the **visible toggle + the inline activity-bubble render defer to PT.1**, where the first real tool + real egress make them meaningful (the loop keeps a no-op `onActivity` seam); (iii) the plan's loop sketch used the **cumulative** assistant text as each round's message content → **duplicates prior-round text** across a multi-round resume; fixed with a per-round `roundText` (cumulative kept only for the persisted body — golden-tested). ## Phase P-Sources — first-class multi-source papers (plan approved 2026-07-05)

> Approved by the Co-Founder ("approve and include PS.2, take your time — make the implementations and related
> surfaces rich and sophisticated") + the per-host rate-limiter reversal (HUMAN.md §1). Planned via an Ultracode
> pass (5 mappers + live API research → 3 designs → a 3-lens adversarial judge panel [migration-risk · scope/demand
> · red-line/coherence] → synthesis) **+ a personal adversarial validation** that grounded the load-bearing premise
> at file:line: **`papers.id` is an opaque `TEXT` PK (`PaperEntity.kt:17`), so multi-source identity is additive
> columns with ZERO rows re-keyed — the scariest migration is designed out, not attempted.** Governed by
> **`docs/SPEC-P-SOURCES.md`**. **Thesis:** P-Tools lets the model *find* chemRxiv/S2 papers but a non-arXiv hit is
> **read-only** (identity is arXiv-keyed); P-Sources makes it a **first-class citizen** — import → **read its PDF**
> → organize — closing the HUMAN.md §3 carve-out. **Committed cut = PS.0 + PS.1 + PS.2** (PS.3 demand-gated). The
> LaTeXML HTML reader stays arXiv-only (it doesn't generalize); **PDF + abstract is the coherent floor** for every
> other source. Every new egress host is user-approved; arXiv keeps its ≥3s limiter singleton (structurally
> enforced) while non-arXiv hosts get their own ~1.2s polite mutex.

- [x] **PS.0 — Source-identity abstraction + additive schema (dark, no user-visible change).** A narrow `PaperRef`
  seam + `Source` enum in `core/model` (`ArxivRef` + one generic `ExternalRef` — **no** speculative per-source
  subclasses or resolver ladder); `PaperEntity` +`origin`(`DEFAULT 'arxiv'`)/`native_id`; **`MIGRATION_6_7`**
  (purely additive `ALTER … ADD COLUMN`, DB `VERSION=7`, KSP `7.json`) + `Migration6To7Test` (identity-hash gate +
  an explicit **zero-rows-re-keyed** assertion, Robolectric in `test` so CI runs it); `PaperMappers` map
  `ref`↔`storageId`/`origin`/`native_id`; `Paper.id: ArxivId → ref: PaperRef` behind a temporary shim deleted
  incrementally to keep every commit green. **Ruling:** a NEW `origin` column — **NOT** overloading the existing
  `papers.source` provenance enum (`EmbeddingDao` filters `source != 'S2_STUB'` — the anti-repurpose lesson).
  Un-prefixed id ⇒ arXiv; only new non-arXiv rows are namespaced (`chemrxiv:…`). **DoD:** build green; nothing
  dispatches to a non-arXiv branch yet.

  send-to-Claude for non-arXiv, `canonicalUrl()` share, origin-dispatched metadata; organize/on-device search **zero

  v1 round-trip tests; redaction walls green). **Adversarial-found + closed (judges missed):** multi-select dispatch

  bio→date/category feed via `api.biorxiv.org`); `follows.origin` column + `(type,value)`→`(origin,type,value)`

  `categories`). bioRxiv has **no keyword search** (live-confirmed) — follows are category/date only; keyword
  discovery routes through the shipped S2 bridge. Built only if PS.1/PS.2 device usage proves demand.
- [x] **CHECKPOINT P-Sources** (gated after the committed cut PS.0+PS.1+PS.2): **green `./gradlew build` +
  `ktlintCheck`** on merged `main` (PS.2 #106 CI + a genuine `--rerun-tasks` build both green). **Migration

  byte-match `7.json`) is byte-untouched, no `fallbackToDestructiveMigration`. **Red-line audit (structural/unit,
  all green):** every non-arXiv fetch host-gated + self-spacing (`PdfHostPolicyTest` arXiv `assertSame` singleton +
  chem/bio/med `assertNotSame`; `AllowedHostsInterceptorTest` off-host redirect fails closed per-hop;
  `AllowedHosts.isAllowedUrl` https+host gate); arbitrary-host OA `importable:false`+not-cached + de-dup no-fork

  untouched; backup redaction green (`BackupManagerTest`); `:core:* ∌ :app`; no telemetry dep. **End-to-end per

  universal-DOI + R1-synthesis capstones deferred). **Bonus:** the intermittent `:app` Robolectric flake was
  root-caused + eliminated across all 18 Room suites this phase. Ticked in its own `checkpoint: P-Sources` commit.
