# Phase P-Feeds — multi-source discovery engine (in-house, native + OpenAlex plug-in)

> Plan approved 2026-07-06 (full Ultracode ritual: live spike + research workflow → 3 Explore maps → personal
> adversarial validation). Governed by **`docs/SPEC-P-FEEDS.md`**. **Reframe:** this session's live research found
> the shipped **chemRxiv search (PT.4) is broken in production** — `chemrxiv.org`'s API is Cloudflare
> fingerprint-gated (curl AND the app's real OkHttp both get a synthetic 404; every wrapper abandoned direct
> access). **OpenAlex** (`api.openalex.org`, un-gated) re-serves chemRxiv/bio/med/arXiv + many sources we lack.
> **Decision (Co-Founder): a HYBRID in-house multi-source engine** — each source uses its best backend, OpenAlex
> as one pluggable backend (not wholesale): native arXiv (Atom) + native bio/med (`api.biorxiv.org`, un-gated,
> server-side category, fresh, un-metered) + OpenAlex for chemRxiv (CF-dead direct) + new sources (Research
> Square/SSRN/Preprints.org/PsyArXiv). Fixes chemRxiv discovery, adds cross-source follows, unlocks new sources,
> + an optional BYOK OpenAlex key. chemRxiv PDF stays **external-open** (Atypon cookie-wall, verified). Red lines
> hold: new hosts host-gated + self-spacing (never the ≥3s arXiv singleton), host-gated importability fails
> closed, BYOK key in EncryptedSharedPreferences, no telemetry, no destructive migration.

- [x] **PF.0 — `OpenAlexClient` + BYOK plumbing + host (foundation, no user-facing change).** New
  `core/network/openalex/OpenAlexClient.kt` on the `@ArxivClient` host-gated client (own 1.2s mutex, `AppResult`
  mapping) — `search`/`browse` (cursor-paginated) + DTOs that normalize OpenAlex's quirks (URL-prefixed
  `id`/`doi`/`source.id` stripped; the **inverted-index abstract** reconstructed to plain text; often-null
  `best_oa_location.pdf_url` → read-only). Free polite-pool via a `mailto` param + optional per-request BYOK
  `apiKey` supplier → `?api_key=`. `AllowedHosts` +`api.openalex.org` +`api.biorxiv.org`. `ProviderId.OPENALEX` +
  DI provider (key from `AiKeyVault`). **Tests:** `OpenAlexClientTest` 7/7 — golden-decodes a **real** captured
  chemRxiv fixture (inverted-index abstract + prefix-strip), MockWebServer URL/cursor/BYOK params, error mapping.
- [x] **PF.1 — fix chemRxiv search via OpenAlex + honest disclosure (the correctness win).** `search_chemrxiv`
  now discovers via `OpenAlexClient` filtered to the chemRxiv source id (its own API is Cloudflare-dead) —
  `okOpenAlexChemSearch` maps each work → the existing `ChemHitDto`/`ExternalPaperDraft` (reconstructed abstract,
  stripped DOI), **host-gated importability** (`AllowedHosts.isAllowedUrl` on the OA PDF — chemrxiv.org →
  importable, an off-host/`doi.org` OA url → read-only). **Honest egress:** the tool + its activity-bubble string
  now name `api.openalex.org`; the tool-desc notes the PDF may open-in-browser (cookie-wall). `ChemRxivClient`
  kept in-tree but **unwired** (documented CF-dead). Reuses the PS.1/PS.2 import seam verbatim. Tests:
  `ToolRegistryTest` chemRxiv-via-OpenAlex (mapping, limit-clamp+source-filter, import+de-dup, fail-closed
  no-PDF/off-host-PDF); `ToolPackageNoOkHttpStructuralTest` green.
- [x] **PF.2 — native bio/med backend (`BioRxivApiClient`) + `PreprintBackend` engine + `follows.origin` v7→v8.**
  New `core/network/biorxiv/BioRxivApiClient.kt` on the `@ArxivClient` host-gated client (own 1.2s mutex) hitting
  `api.biorxiv.org/details/{server}/{start}/{end}/{cursor}/json?category=` — DTOs decode the API's quirks (`total`
  is a **string**, `authors` a **semicolon-joined** string). The `PreprintBackend` interface + `PreprintHit`/
  `PreprintPage` + `PreprintBackendRegistry` land now (rule-of-two: `BioRxivBackend` + `OpenAlexBackend`).
  `BioRxivBackend` maps each item → a hit with a **deterministic, host-allowlisted** PDF url
  (`www.{server}.org/content/{doi}v{version}.full.pdf`) + an integer-offset cursor; `OpenAlexBackend` wraps
  `OpenAlexClient.browse` (sid-mapped, host-gated OA PDF). **Room v7→v8** — additive `follows.origin` (default
  `'arxiv'`) + unique index `(type,value)`→`(type,value,origin)` (`Migration7To8` + KSP-generated `8.json`).
  `FollowSyncWorker` dispatches on `follow.origin`: arXiv → native Atom (unchanged), else → its `PreprintBackend`
  (paginated, DOI-deduped, first-sync-windowed) → the origin-blind inbox pipeline. **Tests:** `Migration7To8Test`
  (identity-hash + `'arxiv'` backfill + widened index), `BioRxivClientTest` (golden fixture decode + URL params +
  error map + backend synthesized-PDF/cursor), `OpenAlexBackendTest` (works→hits, source+date filter, unmapped
  source fails), `FollowSyncWorkerTest` origin-branch (a biorxiv follow rides the backend into the inbox);
  structural `NoDirectNewCall` +`/biorxiv/` self-spaced exception. Green `./gradlew build`.
- [x] **PF.3 — chemRxiv + new-source follows via OpenAlex + source/category follow-picker UI.** Added 4 additive
  `Source` values (Research Square/SSRN/Preprints.org/PsyArXiv — no migration; `BY_PREFIX` auto-derives) routed to
  `openAlexBackend` (exhaustive `OpenAlexClient.sidFor` kills the old silent `else→null`). OpenAlex browse gained an
  **OpenAlex Field** category filter (`primary_topic.field.id:fields/N`, live-verified Chemistry=16; wrong id fails
  safe count=0; whole-source stays byte-identical). Static, 0-credit vocab tables (`OpenAlexFields.kt` 26 Fields,
  `BioRxivCategories.kt` 27 bio/46 med byte-exact) + a `PreprintSourceRegistry`. **Origin-aware follow lifecycle**
  (the load-bearing fix): `FollowDao.delete(type,value,origin)`; `CategoryRepository.setCategoryFollowed(...,source)`
  writes `origin=wire` + cleans inbox on unfollow (`InboxDao.deleteByFollowId`); grid query scoped `origin='arxiv'`;
  **Today `hasFollows` decoupled** to an origin-agnostic count (non-arXiv-only followers no longer see the wrong
  empty state); **backup carries `origin`** (additive, no schema bump). A `SourceFollowSheet` picker in Explore
  (source chips → whole-source + category toggles, `(origin,value)`-keyed, light/dark previews, TalkBack). Firehose
  paging short-circuits on the page-1 first-sync fill (credit budget). New-source PDFs stay host-gated → external-open.
  **Tests:** SourceTest (wire round-trip), FollowDaoTest (cross-origin delete/observe/count), InboxDaoTest
  (deleteByFollowId), CategoryRepositoryTest (origin-aware + inbox cleanup), OpenAlexClient/BackendTest (Field
  clause + byte-identical no-category), OpenAlexSidTableTest (SID↔routing invariant), PreprintSourceRegistryTest
  (26-Field pin + vocab), FollowSyncWorkerTest (firehose short-circuit), BackupManagerTest (origin round-trip +
  no-origin back-compat + index-discriminates), AllowedHostsTest (new hosts read-only). Green `./gradlew build`.
- [x] **PF.4 — optional BYOK OpenAlex key (Settings card, mirrors S2).** A standalone optional-key card in the
  AI-provider Settings (`OpenAlexKeySection`), mirroring the PT.3 S2 card: write-only masked entry → `AiKeyVault`
  under `ProviderId.OPENALEX` (EncryptedSharedPreferences), sent as `?api_key=` by the already-wired supplier
  (`AppModule` PF.0); free-by-default `mailto` polite pool; **no Test button, no default radio** (OpenAlex backs
  discovery/follows, not chat). Copy explains the per-device free budget + when a key helps. `saveOpenAlexKey`/
  `clearOpenAlexKey` on the VM (+`openAlexKeyConfigured` state). **Tests:** VM round-trip (trims, configures,
  never becomes the chat default, clears). Key never touches DB/logs/backups (same red line as S2). Green build.
- [x] **CHECKPOINT P-Feeds** — green build + ktlint; migration integrity (`Migration7To8Test` + `8.json` +
  zero-rows); red-line audit (backends host-gated + self-spacing, arXiv singleton untouched, `data/tool`
  okhttp-free, host-gated importability fail-closed, backup/BYOK redaction, `:core:* ∌ :app`, no telemetry);
  per-source e2e; `VERIFICATION.md` device items; docs current. Committed cut PF.0–PF.2; expansion PF.3–PF.4.
  **Verified 2026-07-06:** `./gradlew build` green (CI runs #110–#112 all green first-try — the flake was killed
  in PF.3 via `sqliteMode=NATIVE`). Red-line audit re-run at the phase boundary: `NoDirectNewCallStructuralTest`
  + `/biorxiv/`,`/openalex/` self-spaced exceptions green (arXiv ≥3s singleton untouched); `ToolPackageNoOkHttp`
  green; egress allowlist = exactly {arXiv group, s2, chemrxiv.org, www.bio/medrxiv.org, api.openalex.org,
  api.biorxiv.org, huggingface.co} — no new-source PDF hosts (read-only, deferred); no telemetry deps; no
  `:core:*`→`:app` import; `Migration7To8Test` identity-hash + zero-rows-re-keyed; `8.json` committed (51 KB);
  no destructive migration; the OpenAlex BYOK key touches only `EncryptedSharedPreferences` (never DB/backup/logs).
  Per-source discovery/follow e2e is CI-golden-tested (arXiv native, bio/med `api.biorxiv.org`, chemRxiv+new
  OpenAlex). **Device-bound e2e deferred to a session** (`VERIFICATION.md` B1a/B1b + the chemRxiv/bio-med PDF
  checks) — never blocks `[x]`. **P-Feeds is complete.** Deferred upside tracked in the backlog + `HUMAN.md`.

## Phase P4 — Smarter discovery: two-sided inbox ranker (plan approved 2026-07-06)

> Approved by the Co-Founder (steer: "proceed with on-device inbox ranking … dismiss-negatives + follows-cold-start
> + explicit thumbs; let planning weigh centroid-vs-classifier"). Planned via an Ultracode pass (4-agent map → 3
> designs → adversarial stress + a completeness/harvest critic → synthesis) **+ a personal adversarial validation**
> that grounded every load-bearing claim at file:line — including the **premise correction** that the positive-only
> ranker ALREADY ships and runs live (`EmbeddingWorker.scoreInbox` + `SyncScheduler` 6h/manual + `TodayScreen`
> "Likely relevant"), so this phase **deepens** it, not rebuilds it. Governed by **`docs/SPEC-SEARCH.md` §5**.
> **Thesis:** the shipped scorer is arxiv-sanity's *positive-only* half — it discards the dismiss signal and gives a
> follows-only user (<10 library) pure recency. P4 completes the two-sided idea on the existing zero-egress bge
> substrate: **dismiss-as-negative** (Rocchio push-away) + **follows-as-cold-start-seed** + an **explicit thumbs**
> up/down signal, all on-device. **Model ruling: Rocchio two-sided centroid, NOT an on-device classifier** — it
> reuses `KMeans`, stays deterministic, keeps the score in `[0,1]` (so `RELEVANT_THRESHOLD=0.55` + `ScoreBar`
> survive) and degrades to today's exact behavior with no negatives; the logistic/SVM classifier is **deferred**
> (backlog, gated on this phase's label table). **Scope: ranker-deepening only** — the P4-line's "more like
> this"/author-following/trending clauses stay deferred.

- [x] **P4.0 — Durable feedback schema + Rocchio math core (dark, no user-visible change).** New durable
  `paper_feedback` table (`paper_id` PK → `papers` CASCADE, `signal`/`source`/`created_at`) +
  `PaperFeedbackEntity`/`PaperFeedbackDao` (upsert-REPLACE, `negativePaperIds`/`positivePaperIds`/`voteFor`/`clear`);
  **`MIGRATION_8_9`** (additive `CREATE TABLE`, DB `VERSION=9`, KSP `9.json`) + `Migration8To9Test` (identity-hash
  gate + additive/paper-survives + table-usable). Pure **`RocchioRanker`** in `:core:search`
  (`clamp01(α·maxCosine(pos) − γ·cosine(neg))`, `α=1.0`/`γ=0.5`, `NEG_MIN=3`) + a shared `internal` **`VectorMath`**
  (`meanVector`/`l2Normalized`) that `KMeans` now reuses (removing its private duplicates, reusing `dotSimilarity`) —
  one shared copy, no drift. `RocchioRankerTest`: no-negatives ≡ `similarityToNearest` (bit-identical), dismiss-cluster
  < save-cluster, output ∈ [0,1], deterministic, graceful at <3 negatives. Behind the pipeline — `scoreInbox` **not
  yet switched**. DoD: green `./gradlew build`; no device surface.
- [x] **P4.1 — Wire the two-sided scorer + follows cold-start seed.** Extracted the scoring logic out of
  `EmbeddingWorker` into an injectable **`InboxScorer`** (real-DAO testable, no ML/download mocking) — the worker now
  delegates via `inboxScorer.scoreInbox { isStopped }`. `InboxScorer` builds pos/neg centroids from `paper_feedback`
  + library (**model-guarded**: a stale-model/wrong-dim vector is skipped, guarding a `dot()` crash), injects a
  negative-excluded follows seed (`InboxDao.activeIdsFromEnabledFollows` join) *before* the `<10`-library cold-start
  gate (fixing zero-personalization-with-follows without regressing the ≥10 path), and scores via `RocchioRanker`.
  `InboxRepository.dismiss()` snapshots the negative into `paper_feedback` (survives `pruneDismissed`); a new
  `undoDismiss` clears it so an undone dismiss is complete (VM `undo` routes DISMISSED→`undoDismiss`). SPEC-SEARCH
  §5/§7 rewrite (two-sided + cold-start + reverse "no feedback UI in v1" + "weekly"→"~6h/manual"), SPEC-DATA §2
  (+ realized-migrations self-heal v4→v9), VERIFICATION `B2a`. Tests: `InboxScorerTest` (dismiss demotes below a save,
  cold-start-with-follows yields scores, disabled-follow/empty-profile stays null, stale-model skipped) +
  `TodayViewModelTest`/`InboxTriageUndoTest` dismiss→undo label round-trip. Green `./gradlew build`.
- [x] **P4.2 — Explicit thumbs (relevance vote) feedback signal.** Storage + plumbing:
  `InboxRepository.setRelevanceVote(up)` toggles `paper_feedback(source='thumb', ±1)` (tap the set direction to
  clear); `TodayViewModel.relevanceVote`; `InboxPaper.vote` surfaced **reactively** (the `observeActiveInbox` query
  gained a `LEFT JOIN paper_feedback … source='thumb'` → the row updates the instant the label changes). UI: an
  opt-in `onVote`/`vote` slot on `PaperListItem` (→ `SwipeablePaperRow`), rendered as a `RelevanceVoteButtons`
  thumb-up/down pair — coexists with the save/dismiss swipes (both gestures were taken → thumbs are buttons). **The
  Co-Founder chose row-level placement** (this session). Two adopted UX calls (HUMAN §1, overridable): **thumb-down
  is a SOFT "less like this"** — it demotes next pass but keeps the paper in the inbox (distinct from dismiss's
  removal); and **no per-tap snackbar** — the filled/outline icon state is the confirmation (state-aware TalkBack
  descriptions announce it), which is cleaner than a snackbar on a visible toggle. Strings added with consumers;
  light+dark previews; `PreviewFixtures` gains `vote`. Tests: `TodayViewModelTest` thumb toggle (up→clear→down) +
  the dismiss/undo label round-trip; backup redaction wall extended with `feedback`/`vote`/`signal`/`relevance`
  (the schema-pin + descriptor-tree tests already prove `paper_feedback` can't leak). Green `./gradlew build`.
- [x] **CHECKPOINT P4** — full `./gradlew build` green on merged `main` (P4.0+P4.1+P4.2); migration v8→v9 tested
  (`Migration8To9Test` identity-hash) + `9.json` committed, additive/no destructive; **red-line audit green** —
  the ranker is fully on-device (`InboxScorer`/`RocchioRanker` have zero okhttp/rate-limiter/logging; scoring
  touches only local Room DAOs + pure math), `paper_feedback` is local-only (grep-confirmed absent from
  `BackupManager`/`LibraryExporter`; the backup schema-pin + descriptor-tree + P4-extended forbidden-name tests
  enforce it), no telemetry deps added, `:core:* ∌ :app` (structurally enforced by the green build);
  VERIFICATION `B2a` + `L7` recorded; SPEC-SEARCH §5/§7 + SPEC-DATA §2 (+ v4→v9 realized-migrations self-heal) +
  HUMAN §1/§2/§3 self-heals landed. Checked in its own commit `checkpoint: phase P4`.

## Phase P-Dispatch — source-aware routine payloads (plan approved 2026-07-07)

> Approved by the Co-Founder (the first "harvested opportunity" after P4; the loose-ends sweep stays queued after
> this + the cross-source-polish / classifier opportunities). Planned via an Ultracode Workflow (3-agent map → 3
> designs → 3 adversarial stress passes → completeness critic → synthesis; all 11 agents succeeded, the stress
> passes caught real errors — an `edgesAmong` method mix-up, a `toDomain`→`toListDomain` compile blocker, an
> S2_STUB neighbor-leak regression) **+ a personal adversarial validation** grounding the load-bearing claims at
> file:line. Governed by **`docs/SPEC-CLAUDE-BRIDGE.md`**. **Thesis:** dispatch is arXiv-only — `DispatchRepository`
> filters non-arXiv papers out (`:265`), the send action is hidden for them (`PaperDetailScreen.kt:193`), and the
> builder would *crash* on a non-arXiv `Paper` (`Payload.kt` read the `paper.id` shim, `error()` at `Paper.kt:42`)
> — so after P-Feeds/P-Sources you still can't send a chemRxiv/bio/med paper to a Claude routine. P-Dispatch makes
> payloads source-aware **additively**: arXiv payloads stay byte-identical under `arxiver/v1`; a non-arXiv paper
> rides four optional keys (`source`/`native_id`/`url`/`pdf_fetchable`) with `arxiv_id`/`abs_url`/`version` absent.
> **Schema ruling: additive, no `arxiver/v2` bump** — a v2 cut would strand every existing arXiv routine for zero
> capability additive can't deliver; single-user, so the only residual is "your own routine must handle the new
> shape if you send it non-arXiv papers."

- [x] **PD.1 — Source-aware wire shape + source-safe builder (dark, no runtime change).** `PayloadPaper`/
  `PayloadNeighbor` gain nullable-additive `source`/`native_id`/`url`/`pdf_fetchable` (declared between
  `citation_count` and `user` so an arXiv payload serializes byte-identically — the new keys vanish under
  `explicitNulls=false`). `PayloadBuilder.toPayloadPaper` rewritten off `paper.ref` (`as? ArxivRef` /
  `canonicalUrl()` / `pdfUrl`), retiring the crashing `paper.id` shim read: arXiv branch byte-identical, non-arXiv
  branch source-correct, never throws on an `ExternalRef`. New `Paper.isPdfFetchable()` = `ref is ArxivRef`
  (conservative/honest; bio/med under-promised, host-refinement backlogged). The `DispatchRepository` arXiv-only
  filter STAYS in place — nothing ships behaviorally (coupled-safety PR). Tests: the existing all-arXiv golden
  passes **unchanged** (additivity proof) + a non-arXiv golden (null-tolerant accessors) + a mixed-selection
  byte-identity golden + redaction re-run with a non-arXiv paper. Green `./gradlew build`.
- [x] **PD.2 — Un-gate dispatch (`:app`).** Removed the arXiv-only filter in `DispatchRepository.buildPayload`
  (+ its stale `PS.2` comment); source-aware neighbors via `row.paper.toListDomain().canonicalUrl()` (the
  `toDomain`→`toListDomain` compile fix) with `arxiv_id`/`abs_url` for arXiv and `source`/`url` for non-arXiv;
  an **empty-`url` drop guard** (a non-arXiv paper with no DOI + blank `pdfUrl` is dropped → `NothingToDispatch`);
  un-hid the send action (`PaperDetailScreen.kt:193`, keeping the still-used `Source` import); made the
  `NothingToDispatch` copy cause-neutral. New `DispatchRepositoryTest` (via the public `previewPayload`):
  chemRxiv-only now builds (was 0 → `NothingToDispatch`) source-aware / mixed / link-less-dropped / partial-miss /
  a chemRxiv neighbor gets `source`+`url` while an S2_STUB neighbor is excluded. **Deviations from the plan (all
  better/simpler):** the `deep_dive` caveat → **PD.3** as a *static* template softening (the per-paper
  `pdf_fetchable` flag already signals it; mutating a user-edited instruction at runtime was invasive);
  `NothingToDispatch` copy **kept hardcoded** (cause-neutral) to match its three sibling error strings in the same
  VM (externalizing one of four is inconsistent, and the app's `HardcodedText` lint doesn't flag VM literals); the
  `edgesAmong` "origin-gated" error was in the planning map, **not** the code (no code comment to fix); the
  `source != S2_STUB` neighbor filter is kept as **intent/defense** (a stub can't actually be a neighbor — stubs
  are never embedded, so never in `related_papers` — the test proves the filter via a hand-inserted stub edge).
  Green `./gradlew build`.
- [x] **PD.3 — Narrative + spec + governance.** `DispatchEnvelope` now labels each paper source-aware
  (`arxivId?.let { "arXiv:$it" } ?: "$source:$nativeId"` — **kills `arXiv:null`**) + rewrote the payload prose with
  an unconditional source discriminator + honest `pdf_fetchable` guidance. `DispatchEnvelopeTest` gains a chemRxiv
  case (labelled `chemrxiv:<doi>`, no `arXiv:null`); the "14 papers" count is scoped to the JSON fence (the prose
  now names `arxiv_id`). SPEC-CLAUDE-BRIDGE §3.1/§4/§4.1 rewritten (non-arXiv `papers[]` example, the discriminator
  note, the additive-judgment record, `pdf_fetchable` framed as routine-side capability) + self-healed the example
  `published`/`updated` to the **actual** ISO-instant form. HUMAN.md carve-out resolved + naive-routine-risk row;
  VERIFICATION.md §G device items. **Deviation:** the `deep_dive` **template softening was deferred to backlog** —
  it's starter-text for *new* routine setups only (existing routines are unaffected), the per-paper `pdf_fetchable`
  flag + envelope prose already carry the signal at dispatch time, and changing it forces a `CATALOG_VERSION` bump
  + catalog-golden churn (disproportionate for a future-only, already-covered nicety). Green `./gradlew build`.
- [x] **CHECKPOINT P-Dispatch** — full `./gradlew build` green on merged `main` (PD.1+PD.2+PD.3); goldens green —
  the arXiv golden passes **unchanged** (byte-identity/additivity proof) alongside the new non-arXiv + mixed
  goldens; **red-line audit green** — no token value ever enters the payload/envelope (grep-confirmed: the only
  `token` in `:core:claude` is the ping's explanatory prose), source identity carries only public metadata
  (DOI/`doi.org` URL), user notes/tags stay structurally redacted with a non-arXiv paper in the mix, no telemetry,
  `:core:* ∌ :app` (Payload/DispatchEnvelope stay pure in `:core:claude`, structurally enforced); SPEC-CLAUDE-BRIDGE
  §3.1/§4/§4.1 + ROADMAP + HUMAN self-heals landed. Checked in its own commit `checkpoint: phase P-Dispatch`.

## Phase P5 — Calibrated, measurable inbox relevance (refined plan approved 2026-07-10)

> Researched under Opus (13-agent workflow + web research), then **reviewed and refined post-P-Explorer at the
> Co-Founder's instruction** (8-agent refinement workflow + tech-lead file:line verification). The refinement
> caught **two defects in the original plan** — a label reader that would have said "insufficient data" forever
> (saves never write feedback rows) and stale-embedder machinery referencing a paper-level wipe that didn't exist —
> plus the mixed-quality embedding axis P-Explorer created (SSRN ~100% / recent RS ~86% abstract-stripped →
> title-only vectors through the same 0.55 cut). Locked Co-Founder decisions: the learned head is GATED (a PR the
> harness earns); "Likely relevant" becomes top-k by calibrated score; centroid shrinkage promoted to its own
> subphase. Working plan: the plan file + `p5_refined.md` (session scratchpad). Migration budget: **v13→v14** (P5.3).

- [x] **P5.1 — Offline eval harness** (`:core:search/eval`, pure, dark; ships in RELEASE — P5.4's β-auto-revert
  depends on it on user hardware; only the readout card is debug-gated). `RankerEval`: time-split primary +
  stratified 5-fold above the floor (cost bound ≤6 k-means rebuilds, test-pinned); **Kish-ESS floors (≥15/class),
  not raw rows**; PU-weighted (dismiss 0.3); **segmented on the causal axis `abstract = ''`** with a test proving
  a flat aggregate cannot hide a degraded title-only segment; fold contract closes all three leakage paths incl.
  the cold-start-seed re-entry; seeded bootstrap CI over frozen fold outputs; ECE only ≥50 labels (Brier below);
  **regime honesty** = any fold that ran a different regime than the production model flags the report (the
  original >30%-of-folds rule was DEAD CODE — the ESS floor makes k-fold train sides unable to straddle the
  gates; caught by writing the test). `PaperFeedbackDao.labeledExamples(modelTag)` **UNIONs library saves**
  (defect 1); `EmbeddingDao.clearMarksForModelMismatch` + paper-level `deleteByModelMismatch` at worker start
  (defect 2 — without it a MODEL_NAME bump leaves the feed permanently unranked); `InboxDao.activeScoresBySegment`
  feeds the label-free per-segment distribution tripwire; `RankerEvalRunner` (once per worker pass, never fails
  the worker) publishes to an in-memory `RankerEvalState`; debug-only `RankerHealthCard` in Settings; an
  eval-package NoOkHttp structural test. Tests: `RankerEvalTest` ×9, `PaperFeedbackDaoTest` +5, structural ×1.
- [x] **P5.2 — Positive-centroid shrinkage.** `RocchioRanker.shrinkCentroids` (nearest-shrunken-centroid toward
  the centroids' mean, re-normalized; **λ=0 returns the same list instance** — bit-identity by construction).
  **λ is a per-user selection RULE, never a constant:** `RankerEval.selectShrinkage` picks from the pre-registered
  grid {0, .1, .2, .3} by pooled k-fold AUC and **confirms the winner on the temporally-disjoint time split**
  (selection and confirmation on different splits = the multiplicity guard); 0 below the ESS floor. **Zero extra
  k-means rebuilds** — shrinkage re-scores each fold's already-built centroids, so the ≤6-rebuild cost bound
  holds across the whole grid. Applied live via an in-memory `RankerTuning` (@Singleton, default 0; durable
  tuning arrives with P5.3's `relevance_model`); the worker runs the eval BEFORE scoring so a fresh selection
  applies same-run. Tests: λ=0 instance-identity; shrink-toward-mean + unit-norm; below-floor→0; grid membership;
  the confirmation invariant (a returned λ never tanks the pooled AUC).
- [x] **P5.3 — Per-user calibrated threshold + top-k section.** Additive **v13→v14**: single-row `relevance_model`
  (calibration a/b + shrinkage λ + label counts + NULLABLE head-weights blob — P5.4 needs no second migration;
  single-row invariant in the DAO, **never seeded**: absent ≡ below-floor ≡ exactly 0.55, so fresh and migrated
  installs behave identically) + `paper_feedback.score_at_label` (the D14 exposure-context call — captured at
  label time on dismiss/thumb, NULL for pre-v14 labels, never invented). **`PlattCalibration`** fits σ(a·s+b) by
  deterministic weighted Newton on the harness's **held-out** outputs (train-side scores would inherit their
  optimism), with Platt's smoothed targets (a separable set can't push a→∞), a ≥50-label + ≥10-negative-ESS floor
  (below it: null → the legacy 0.55 EXACTLY), and an **anti-predictive rejection** (a≤0 would invert the section).
  **`tuneAndEvaluate`** = the single production entry: ONE set of fold builds yields λ + the tuned report + the
  calibration inputs (the ≤6-rebuild bound covers the whole pipeline). The RAW score stays what
  `inbox_items.score` persists; Platt is monotone, so Today translates the p=0.5 point ONCE into a raw-score cut
  (live via `relevance_model` observe-flow) — ordering never reshuffles. **"Likely relevant" is now TOP-K (10)**
  above the calibrated floor (the Co-Founder's stable-count decision). Stale-embedder discard on the model row
  mirrors the vector-tag guard. Backup wall extended (calibration/shrinkage/head_weights in the descriptor
  blocklist). Tests: `PlattCalibrationTest` ×5, `Migration13To14Test` (identity hash + sqlite_master DDL equality
  + never-seeded + NULL exposure for old labels), `TodayViewModelTest` +2 (absent row ⇒ exactly 0.55; a=10,b=−4 ⇒
  cut 0.4), `InboxTriageUndoTest` +1 (dismiss stamps the seen score), `BackupManagerTest` blocklist.
- [!] **P5.4 — GATED learned logistic head** (~385 params, pure Kotlin; β auto-→0 whenever the blend fails to
  beat pure Rocchio per-segment on held-out data; gates on ≥8-10 REAL explicit negatives). **Ships only if P5.1
  proves Rocchio leaves precision on the table.** `[needs-user/device]` — the gate's evidence is the
  **Co-Founder's real-profile harness numbers** (VERIFICATION B2b protocol). **Adjudicated 2026-07-10 (Ultracode
  workflow + personal adversarial validation):** the gate is *irreducibly* `[needs-user/device]` — the workflow's
  two validity passes converged on the finding that **no emulator-synthetic profile can CLOSE this gate** (taxonomy-
  proxy labels are a different label-generating process from organic preference, and are partly encoded in the very
  bge geometry being ranked ⇒ a synthetic NO-GO is weak evidence, a synthetic GO only advisory). The full designed
  experiment (an off-device counterfactual logistic-head + LDA + SVM + stacking + paired bootstrap) was **rejected
  as gold-plating** — it would build ~P5.4 itself just to *decide* P5.4 and still couldn't close the gate. What was
  taken instead (zero new production code): a **coherent MODERATE-difficulty emulator readout** replacing the
  useless diffuse AUC-0.50 record — see VERIFICATION B2b. Decision rule unchanged for when the Co-Founder's real
  numbers arrive: healthy AUC + P@10 near ceiling → close no-go (à la PH.8); sufficient data + mediocre precision →
  build it. Synthetic readouts are **advisory only** and never flip this `[!]`.
- [x] **P5.5 — Calibration downgrade hysteresis.** A profile hovering at the calibration-guard boundary (the
  `a≤0`/floor line) used to see Today's "Likely relevant" section flip between the calibrated cut and the legacy-
  0.55 regime across passes. Fixed with **two-pass-confirm on the DOWNGRADE direction only** (`null→fitted` applies
  immediately; `fitted→null` keeps the previous a/b for one pass; two *consecutive* null fits downgrade). Correctness
  needs a persisted counter → **additive v14→v15 migration** (`relevance_model.consecutive_null_fits INTEGER NOT NULL
  DEFAULT 0`, `MIGRATION_14_15`, `15.json`, `Migration14To15Test` — backfill 0 ≡ "current fit is fresh" ≡ pre-P5.5
  semantics). The logic is a pure `resolveCalibrationWrite(previous, fresh, now)` in `RankerEvalRunner`
  (`ResolveCalibrationWriteTest` exhausts the state machine incl. the unreachable half-populated row) + a
  `RankerEvalRunnerTest` integration case pinning the **mixed-vintage row contract** (kept a/b + fittedAt from the
  previous pass; λ + label counts from the fresh pass) across two below-floor passes → downgrade. Backup wall
  extended (`null_fits`/`nullfits` in the descriptor blocklist); the two-pass count is **completed eval passes**, so a
  crash between read and upsert only delays a downgrade, never takes it early or corrupts the streak. Adversarially
  validated (workflow + personal pass): zero fatal, all fixable items folded in. *(Ships stacked on the QW1 PR #141;
  the same-runner coupling is why they land together.)*
- [ ] **CHECKPOINT P5** — full build green ✓ (now through v15); migration identity-hash-tested ✓ (+ a LIVE v3→v14
  eleven-migration upgrade on the emulator, 2026-07-10; v14→v15 identity-hash + DDL tested); red-line audit: zero
  egress from ranking ✓ (airplane-mode ranked the full feed offline, 2026-07-10 emu; NoOkHttp structural scan), no
  new model/host ✓, weights **and the hysteresis streak** never in backups ✓ (the serial-descriptor snapshot guard,
  `null_fits` pinned), no telemetry ✓, `:core:search ∌ :app` ✓ (structural); harness device row ✓ emulator (B2b,
  refreshed 2026-07-10 with the coherent-profile readout) — **holds open pending only the P5.4 disposition**
  (Co-Founder real-profile numbers). *P5.5 device leg (hysteresis persists one pass then downgrades) tracked in
  VERIFICATION B2c — device-only, doesn't block `[x]`.*
  *P5 ledger (recorded):* **[SHIPPED 2026-07-10, QW1]** the debug card's "above cut %" uses the live calibrated cut
  (`RankerEvalRunnerTest` pins both branches) · **[SHIPPED 2026-07-11, P5.5]** the downgrade hysteresis above ·
  B2a's undo-erases-influence + fresh-profile cold-start legs still open (VERIFICATION B2a).

## Phase P-Explorer — complete the multi-source discovery surface (plan approved 2026-07-10)

> **Co-Founder device session (2026-07-10)** found the P-Sources/P-Feeds multi-source expansion is complete at the
> *client* layer but never surfaced in the UI: Explore search is arXiv-only; the follow picker excludes arXiv; every
> OpenAlex-served source shows the same generic 26-Field list (chemRxiv offers "Dentistry"). Asked for a thorough
> audit + a rich, world-class Explorer UX. Planned via an Ultracode Workflow (4 surface maps → gap inventory → 3
> competing IA designs → 3 adversarial stress passes → completeness critic → synthesis) **+ a personal adversarial
> validation** grounding every load-bearing claim at file:line, **+ a 9-agent PDF-host egress probe** (PE.2h).
>
> **Verdict (IA):** Explore becomes one discovery surface where **source is a dimension of the query, not a separate
> app**. Search stays **single-source per submit** (arXiv → native Atom + full filters; each non-arXiv source → one
> metered OpenAlex `search()`), which delivers the reach promise while structurally sidestepping the fan-out tar-pit
> (cross-leg display de-dup, incomparable-rank merge, dual pagination) — fan-out "All sources" is a recorded
> follow-on, not v1. Follows unify into **one Browse-&-Follow directory** with arXiv as a peer row. Library stays
> "my shelf" + a source filter. *Explore = the world, Library = mine.*
>
> **The audit found five latent bugs in shipped code**, independent of the feature request: (1) `SearchViewModel`'s
> `distinctBy { p.id }` `error()`s on any non-arXiv paper (a crash-trap gating all of PE.3); (2) `saveExternalPaper`
> **forks** a cross-posted paper (passes `arxivId=null`, never calls `paperIdByDoi`) — PFP.1 fixed only the
> follow-ingest path, so the *import* path still forks; (3) `paperIdByDoi` matches the **raw** `doi` column while
> callers pass `normalizeDoi(...)` → a `.vN`-versioned DOI silently fails to de-dup; (4) `isPdfFetchable()` was
> `ref is ArxivRef` — *tautologically false* at its only call site (the non-arXiv payload branch), so every
> non-arXiv paper told Claude routines "PDF unfetchable", **including bioRxiv/medRxiv whose PDFs demonstrably fetch**;
> (5) the `primaryCategory` chip renders unguarded while every non-arXiv paper stores `""`.
>
> **PE.2h egress probe verdict (evidence-backed; no new host needed to win):** bio/medRxiv serve `200`, 0 redirects,
> `application/pdf`, `%PDF` on **already-allowlisted** hosts → in-app read is real. chemRxiv is Atypon-cookie-walled
> via an un-allowlisted OIDC hop (shipped browser-open is *correct*). SSRN (ToS bans automated queries) and
> Preprints.org (Akamai edge-deny) are gated → fetching either would circumvent an access control. **PsyArXiv/OSF
> resolves only through `storage.googleapis.com`** — multi-tenant GCS whose bucket is in the URL *path*, so
> exact-host allowlisting cannot scope it to OSF; **granting it would open egress to any bucket → rejected.** The
> standing `assets.chemrxiv.org` HUMAN.md row is **stale** (NXDOMAIN; real PDFs are on the already-allowlisted
> `chemrxiv.org`) → retire + replace it. **We never spoof a browser UA**: bio/medRxiv's robots.txt permits honest
> custom agents, and a blocked honest UA means "no" → degrade to browser.
>
> **Co-Founder decisions:** unified full-screen follow directory · Research Square + Preprints.org keep **all 26**
> Fields (genuine megajournals — curating hides real content); curate only chemRxiv/PsyArXiv/SSRN · investigate all
> PDF hosts now (done) · Research Square **authorized pending an on-device shard check** · chemRxiv in-app read
> **revisited after P-Explorer**.

- [x] **PE.0 — Foundation: provenance + honest fetchability + the crash-trap.** `distinctBy { it.ref.storageId }`
  (bug 1). New `PdfAccess` tier + `Source.pdfAccess()` in `:core:model` (evidence-backed, exhaustive `when`) →
  `Paper.isPdfFetchable()` stops being a tautology, **closing the recorded P-Dispatch `pdf_fetchable`
  host-reachability deferral** (bio/med now honestly `true`; arXiv payload byte-identity untouched — the arXiv
  branch never sets the key). New `PreprintHit.fieldName` threaded from `OpenAlexBackend` (`primary_topic.field`)
  and `BioRxivBackend` (its `category`, already returned, never used) into `Paper.primaryCategory` at ingest
  (bug 5's data side). Structural `PdfAccessAllowlistTest` pins the tier to `AllowedHosts` (an IN_APP source whose
  host isn't allowlisted breaks the build) **and** pins the probe-rejected hosts (`storage.googleapis.com` et al.)
  as permanently un-allowlisted.
- [x] **PE.1 — Per-source curated Field vocabulary, EMPIRICALLY derived** (the reported chemRxiv/"Dentistry"
  incoherence). Rule: offer a Field iff it carries **≥1% of that source's 2024+ works** (measured live via
  `group_by=primary_topic.field.id`, 2026-07-10); curated lists render in **descending real mass**. **The data
  overturned all three intuitive subsets:** chemRxiv → 11 Fields, 95.9% (the "chemistry-adjacent" guess omitted
  **Computer Science 4.68%** + **Medicine 3.85%**); PsyArXiv → 10 Fields, 97.5% (the 3-Field guess omitted
  **Medicine 9.04%** — clinical psych); SSRN → 18 Fields, 96.2% (**the {Econ,Business,Social,Decision} guess covers
  just 27.9% and omits Engineering, its #1 recent Field at 21.87%** — post-Elsevier SSRN is a broad STEM firehose,
  not a law/finance archive). Research Square + Preprints.org → **all 26** (confirmed genuine megajournals: top-10
  covers only ~80–84%, every Field >0.15%). Compile-time; an unknown id now **fails loud** at build.
- [x] **PE.1b — [BUG, FIXED] PsyArXiv lost ~99% of its papers at ingest.** `OpenAlexBackend.toHit` does
  `val d = bareDoi() ?: return null`, but **PsyArXiv is 98.97% DOI-null** (5,498/5,555 — measured 2026-07-10; it is
  OSF-hosted and OpenAlex simply has no DOI for it). So a PsyArXiv follow silently discards nearly everything, and
  PFP.3's health hint then blames the *feed* ("No new papers recently") for the *app's* drop. chemRxiv is 0.00%
  DOI-null, so this is OSF-specific. Re-measured on the *recent* window a follow actually syncs: **340 of 342
  works (99.4%) dropped**. **Fix:** identity falls back to the OpenAlex work id when the DOI is absent
  (`PreprintHit.nativeId` distinct from a now-nullable `doi`), and the paper gets a canonical `landing_url`
  (PsyArXiv is also ~100% `pdf_url`-null, so that URL is its *only* link) — additive migration v12→v13.
  **Correction (self-heal, 2026-07-10):** an earlier note here claimed PsyArXiv's `publication_date` is a
  re-harvest artifact (99% dated 2025) requiring `from_created_date`. **Both halves are false** — I verified
  directly: `from_publication_date:2026-06-26` returns 342 works (a healthy window), and `from_created_date` is
  not a valid OpenAlex filter at all. Acting on that unverified agent claim would have broken PsyArXiv outright.
  Also: PFP.1's DOI de-dup can never match a DOI-less source; SSRN is ~16% DOI-null too.
- [x] **PE.2 — De-dup key correctness + the import-path fork** (bugs 2 & 3). Additive **v11→v12**: `papers.doi_norm`
  (= `normalizeDoi(doi)`), the index re-pointed at it, the now-dead `index_papers_doi` dropped. **Back-filled in
  Kotlin, not SQL** — SQLite has no `REGEXP`, so a pure-SQL backfill could lowercase but never strip a `.vN` suffix,
  i.e. it would leave exactly the rows this migration exists to fix still broken. `doi` stays the verbatim citeable
  value; `doi_norm` is purely the match key, written through the single `Paper.toEntity()` chokepoint so both sides
  of `paperIdByDoi` agree by construction. **`saveExternalPaper` now reuses an existing same-DOI row** instead of
  forking (PFP.1 only ever fixed the follow path; the import seam — reachable from the chat `import_to_library`
  tool — still forked), and deliberately does **not** clobber the richer stored row. Tests: `Migration11To12Test`
  (identity-hash + `.vN` backfill + two-rows-share-a-key anti-brick), `PaperRepositoryTest` ×3 (arXiv row wins,
  versioned-DOI reuse, genuinely-new still creates), `FollowSyncWorkerTest` versioned-DOI regression.
- [x] **PE.3 — Multi-source keyword search.** `Library | arXiv` → `Library | Online`; a **bottom-sheet radio source
  picker** (leftmost chip in either filter bar — a11y over an unreachable chip strip), default arXiv, followed
  sources ★-sorted, browser-only sources honestly captioned. arXiv path byte-untouched (native Atom + full filters);
  each non-arXiv source = **one** `OpenAlexClient.search` per explicit submit, optionally Field-narrowed
  **server-side** (PE.1 vocab; still one call). New `OpenAlexWork.toPaper()` mapper (identity = DOI-else-work-id per
  PE.1b; arXiv cross-post collapses via `resolvePaperRef` AND synthesizes its arXiv pdf url; unreachable hits —
  no doi/landing/pdf — dropped). **Persist-on-interaction** via a new atomic `PaperDao.insertPaperIfAbsentWithRelations`
  (one `@Transaction`: same-ref reuse → `doi_norm` reuse → insert; kills the cacheSearchHit↔FollowSync race);
  `openHit`/`saveHit`/`persistHits` thread the full `Paper` and use the **returned winning id** (reuse can re-key);
  an arXiv cross-post delegates to the cache-first `paper(ref)` so the full native record is stored, not a thin
  shadow. `saveExternalPaper` re-routed through the same DAO chokepoint (one reuse-or-insert seam app-wide).
  **v1 un-paginated (`nextStart=null`)** → the metered auto-load-more is structurally inert; a source switch cancels
  in-flight + clears + never auto-searches; `submittedFilter` nulled on the external branch (a stale arXiv pagination
  snapshot can't page mid-SSRN); `onlineSource` survives process death via `SavedStateHandle`. **Honesty:** external
  count header shows reachable rows (never `meta.count` 12,805 next to 25 rows); "via OpenAlex" caption + a softened
  bio/med lag hint; SSRN/RS abstract-less cards render sanely (guarded chip, detail-screen "No abstract available
  from %s"); BROWSER-tier papers get a direct **Open in browser** detail button (replacing the doomed PDF spinner);
  cancel-rethrow (a source switch never surfaces a ghost error) + **cause-chain-aware `api_key` redaction** at the
  single `Unexpected(...)` chokepoint (also closes a pre-existing browse-path log leak). `launchSingleTop` on the
  paper-detail navigations (a double-tap during persist latency can't stack two entries). Tests: `OpenAlexPaperMapperTest`
  ×6 (golden fixture), `PaperDaoTest` ×3 (atomic chokepoint), `PaperRepositoryTest` ×3 (never-caches-eagerly,
  idempotent, no-clobber winning-id), **`SearchViewModelTest` ×6 — the metering contract proven by counting real
  MockWebServer requests** (source-switch = 0 calls; submit = exactly 1; loadMore = 0; typing = 0; SavedStateHandle
  restore; saveHit FK-safety).
- [x] **PE.4 — Unified Browse-&-Follow directory** (Co-Founder-approved IA). arXiv a peer row with its native
  taxonomy at full-screen real estate; both write seams already exist (`setFollowed`/`setCategoryFollowed`).
  Shipped PR #132 (the split picker is subsumed); emulator-verified 2026-07-10 (VERIFICATION B1a). *(Box healed
  2026-07-10 — PE.0/PE.4 were left `[~]`/`[ ]` when the phase checkpointed; the Decision log had the record.)*
- [x] **PE.5 — Library source dimension.** `LibraryUiState.sourceFilter: Source?` + a second chip row in the
  papers tab that renders **only when the library genuinely spans >1 source** (an all-arXiv library sees zero added
  chrome) and lists **only sources actually present** (never an SSRN chip with no SSRN paper). `presentSources`
  derives from the status-filtered list, so picking a chip can never erase its own row. Tap-again clears. No data
  change (`paper.ref.origin` was already there). `LibraryViewModelTest` pins the filter + presence rules.
- [x] **PE.6 — Docs & deferral sweep.** PRD gains a **Scope-evolution note** (v1.0 was arXiv-scoped by design; the
  shipped product spans the preprint ecosystem, with arXiv the center of gravity and the generalization governed by

  superseded-by-PF.2** (bio/med follows shipped there in generalized form — closed explicitly, not silently). The

  block + PE.3 refinements ledger are in place above.
- [x] **CHECKPOINT P-Explorer** — full `./gradlew build` green on merged `main` (7m31s, post-PE.6). Both new

  committed, no destructive migration. **Red-line audit (evidence-based):** `AllowedHosts.kt` **byte-untouched**

  (the win was fixing code that lied about hosts we already had); OpenAlex metering held by tests counting **real
  MockWebServer requests** (typing 0 · switch 0 · submit exactly 1 · loadMore 0) + un-paginated v1; arXiv ≥3s
  limiter file untouched; zero-network-on-open structural for the directory/picker/vocab; no telemetry deps; no
  `:core:*→:app` import; the OpenAlex client logs nothing + chain-aware `api_key` redaction at its one error
  chokepoint. Device rows staged: B1a (directory), B1e (bio/med in-app PDF), B1f (RS shard — answered from the
  local box), B1g (multi-source search + TalkBack). Docs-only checkpoint commit.
